He carried the decision of Manchukuo and went to Tokyo, where he will begin important negotiations with the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Soviet Ambassador to Japan. It is expected that the joint committee plan will be concretized, and the issue of purchasing the Sino-Eastern Railway will take a sharp turn and be resolved. The content of the highest policy of Manchukuo carried by Deputy Minister Ohashi is said to be roughly as follows: (1) In principle, the Sino-Eastern Railway will be purchased by Manchukuo. The purchase price and payment method will be decided upon careful negotiation between Japan and Manchukuo. (2) An agreement must be signed on the issue of the Joint Committee of Russia, Japan, and Manchukuo to prevent the danger of border conflicts between Russia and Manchukuo, but the opinions of the Soviet Union must be solicited and the borders of the Heilongjiang River, the borders of Man-Manli, and the borders of Suifen should be established. After the League of Nations unanimously passed the non-recognition of the puppet organization, the Soviet Union would not violate the public opinion of the whole world by immediately recognizing the puppet organization. (15th, Central News Agency Telegram)

(Nanjing) After Russian Foreign Minister Litvinov announced that Russia was preparing to sell the Sino-Eastern Railway, our Ministry of Foreign Affairs submitted a serious protest on the 13th, which has not yet been answered. According to outside sources, Karakhan replied to Ambassador Yan on the 9th that Russia had no intention of selling the Sino-Eastern Railway. On the 11th, Li made a completely contradictory statement. The reason for this is that Karakhan and Li have different opinions. Li is not very clear about the situation in the Far East and the interests of selling the railway. Since Li made the statement about selling the railway, the dispatches and comments sent by the diplomatic personnel of various countries stationed in Russia on this matter have been detained by the Russian government. (15th, Central News Agency Telegram)

(Harbin) In view of the fact that bandits are still rampant in the eastern section of the Sino-Eastern Railway, the Director of the Sino-Eastern Railway has instructed the Railway Bureau that night trains shall not be operated on that section in the future. (Harbin) On the 8th, Manchukuo suddenly reassigned important Manchu officials of the Sino-Eastern Railway to refresh the lineup. The future activities of the newly appointed officials are quite noteworthy. (Japanese United Press News)

Soviet Russia Raises 3 Billion in Internal Debt 31

For the Use of the Second Five-Year Plan, All Workers in the Country Must Subscribe

The Movement to Recognize the United States is Again in Full Swing, with Plans to First Conclude a Favorable Trade Agreement with Russia

(Moscow) The Central Executive Committee and the People's Committee of the Soviet Government issued an order today deciding to issue a public debt of 3 billion rubles to be repaid in ten years for the construction of the Second Five-Year Plan. (14th, Special Telegram)

(Moscow) The Soviet government announced today that it will raise an internal debt of 3 billion rubles. According to the debt-raising regulations, all workers and state employees who receive salaries are expected to contribute at least three weeks' salary to the internal debt before the deadline of October 1. This debt is due on October 1, 1943, with an interest rate of 1%. However, it can also be repaid in advance through quarterly lotteries. It is said that this money will be used to expand the government's construction plans and enhance the government's credit. (14th, Special Telegram)

(Washington) Although the issue of the United States joining the International Court of Justice has been temporarily shelved, the issue of recognizing Soviet Russia is currently being processed in the Senate. Since the news of the Soviet Russia raising an internal debt of 3 billion rubles reached the United States, the recognition issue has changed from dormancy to activity. Today, several Democratic senators anticipate that Senator Borah, who has been the strongest advocate for recognition, will submit a proposal to the Senate. According to his friends, the President is prepared to submit a recognition proposal before Congress adjourns. Experts within the State Department have also prepared a report on the possibility of trade with Russia in the next fiscal year. Recently, several lower-level officials of the State Department deeply believe that some of the internal debt raised by Soviet Russia may be used to purchase machinery in the United States. In the past, this type of trade was obtained by Britain and Germany, but in the future, it may be transferred to the American industrial sector. Therefore, the recognition issue has become more prevalent again due to the news of Soviet Russia raising debt. According to reliable sources, the American recognition movement was only delayed because of the recent signs of a break between Russia and Japan over the Sino-Eastern Railway. Borah has investigated the attitude of the senators and has a majority in favor of recognition, as long as a favorable trade agreement can be obtained before fully restoring diplomatic relations. Economic Conflicts of Interest Among Capitalist Countries 34

The London Conference is Bound to Fail | Sharp Observations from Russian Newspapers | Britain, America, and France Seem to Consistently Support Japan

(Moscow) The Pravda newspaper here published an editorial today titled "From Washington to London," discussing the recent conference held in Washington and the World Economic Conference to be held in London next month. The newspaper first stated that the United States' abandonment of the gold standard has knocked the tool of dumping out of the hands of the British Conservative Party. Therefore, on the eve of the Economic Conference, the economic war between Britain and the United States has already taken a sharp form. Since the Great War, the antagonism between Britain and the United States has not reached such intensity and sharpness. Currently, Britain has taken urgent steps to conclude business agreements with Germany, Denmark, and Argentina, with the purpose of ensuring the minimum amount of exports of British goods to these countries. At the same time, the United States uses the war debt issue as its most powerful weapon. The United States now needs allies to stabilize its power in Europe while dealing with the situation in the Far East. The antagonism between Japan and the United States in the Far East has taken a particularly sharp form. However, in the talks between Roosevelt, MacDonald, and Herriot, Britain's attitude towards the Far East issue seems to have consistently supported the aggressors. The newspaper went on to say that the future World Economic Conference will be the same as the Geneva Conference, that is, each side will use the words of pretended peace to cover up the fierce competition of their general staffs. In addition to economic infighting, the preparation of the British and American naval and military forces will also advance in competition. The newspaper concluded that the first act of the Washington Conference has failed. Now they have moved their conference to London, where they will use the fog of the British Isles to cover up their impending conflicts. However, the London Conference is unlikely to succeed. The result will only be an intensification of opposition and conflict. (14th, TASS Telegram)

New Weapons for the League of Nations' Anti-Smoking Campaign 42

The Convention on Limiting Narcotic Drugs to be Implemented on July 9, Establishing an International Mechanism to Supervise the Manufacturing of Each Contracting State

(Geneva) The Chairman of the League of Nations' Anti-Smoking Committee, Bourgeois, issued a memorandum stating that the prohibition of smoking is a difficult and arduous struggle because international private trafficking groups have strong forces. According to investigations, one of these groups was able to profit up to 150,000 pounds in less than half a year. The International Convention on the Limitation of the Manufacture of Narcotic Drugs is a new weapon. The purpose of this convention is not only to bind each country with mutual obligations, but also to organize a real international administration to supervise and supervise the economic relations between the contracting states. Limiting manufacturing includes three main issues: (1) stipulating the quantity of legitimate uses of narcotic drugs in various countries in the world; (2) allocating a certain amount of raw materials to manufacturing countries; (3) allocating to consuming countries according to the number of legitimate needs, and not exceeding the amount. The memorandum also stated that economic panic and the world's economic relations really need to be organized. The new convention on limiting the manufacture of narcotic drugs stipulates layers from raw materials to finished products and is the first model of the world's economic organization. We are thus reminded that the manufacture and sale of arms can also be modeled in this way. The League of Nations Secretariat will publish an important memorandum on this issue this week. (14th, Havas Telegram)

Ju Zheng Reports on the Sino-Eastern Railway Incident 46

At the National Government's Memorial Week

(Nanjing) The National Government held a memorial week for the Premier on the morning of the 15th. On the other hand, we should strive to become stronger, unite from top to bottom, and cure the weakness and stagnation ourselves. We must strive for self-reliance and never again make the illusion of relying on others to prolong our lives. Then our country may be saved. (15th, Central News Agency Telegram)

Central Memorial Week: Shi Qingyang Reports on Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs 47

(Nanjing) The Central Government held its 78th Memorial Week at 8:00 AM on the 15th. Ye Chucang, Wang Qi, Ma Chaojun, Li Ciwen, and approximately 600 other staff members attended. Chairman Ju Zheng presided, and Shi Qingyang delivered a report. He stated that, apart from the coastline, every region along China's borders, from the Three Eastern Provinces through Mongolia, Tibet, Xinjiang, Yunnan, and Guangxi, borders strong neighbors. These regions lack national defense infrastructure and the people are poorly educated, creating a truly perilous situation. Mongolia's political organization has distinct characteristics. It is governed militarily, with people of a certain age incorporated into banners under the command of a Zuoling (Captain) or Canling (Major), headed by a Zhasake-style chief administrator. Several banners form a "Jian" or "Bu," with a Jianzhang (Director) or Deputy Jianzhang to oversee them. "Menggong" (League Chiefs) are publicly elected, while banner chiefs are hereditary. Tibet is governed by religion, with the Dalai Lama holding supreme power. Under him are four "Gabulun" (Cabinet Ministers) managing various affairs. Local areas are divided into sixty-eight "Zong" (districts), each with a "Yingguan" (Military Officer) managing general affairs. Major events in Tibet must be decided through conferences of the three major monasteries: Bipeng, Sera, and Gadan. Mongol and Tibetan society is divided into monks, nobles, commoners, and slaves. Virtually all Mongols and Tibetans are Buddhist. Historically, Mongols and Tibetans valued plunder and warfare, rewarding warriors. Brave and intelligent men invariably became warriors. Buddhist teachings prohibit killing, and the great virtues, scholarship, and profound understanding of eminent monks transformed these murderous and warlike warriors into compassionate and benevolent lamas. Through the support of successive Yuan, Ming, and Qing dynasties, the Mongol and Tibetan peoples have become gentle and amicable. The Qing dynasty's governance of Mongolia and Tibet was based on the principle of "respecting their religion, not altering their customs; standardizing their administration, not changing what is suitable." The Lifan Yuan (Court of Colonial Affairs) was established to oversee tributes and imperial ceremonies. Generals and governors were stationed in Mongolia to supervise the leagues and banners, while vice-resident ministers were stationed in Tibet to oversee major events. Great lamas and princes were treated favorably to maintain their dignity. Our Party and our late Premier taught that all domestic groups should be treated equally to create a single, great Chinese nation. Therefore, the Central Government's policy toward Mongolia and Tibet emphasizes peaceful solutions, expanding opportunities for Mongolians and Tibetans to participate in government, encouraging their youth to study, and treating religious leaders and princes with respect, all aimed at supporting Mongolia and Tibet. The Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission, following these guidelines, is working on popularizing education, liberating slaves, improving the organization of leagues and banners to give people the opportunity to participate in politics, and establishing various production organizations to improve people's livelihoods and skills. These plans have been under consideration for years, but progress has been limited due to funding issues. However, within our means, we have sent representatives to comfort officials in the Chahar and Suiyuan Leagues. We have established a Tibetan Refugee Relief Association in Beiping, requested funds from the Central Government, and solicited donations from charities to help refugees returning from Outer Mongolia. We have also consulted on halting the cultivation of banner lands, relocated the Beiping office to Zhangjiakou, promoted the establishment of a province in Xikang, and continued the peaceful resolution of the Tibetan issue. The situation in Mongolia and Tibet is extremely serious. However, Qingyang believes that two points are even more serious: firstly, the gradual weakening of the old forces and the disunity of the new forces. In recent years, due to the instability of the environment and life, and the agitation of new trends, not only have the respected princes gradually lost the sympathy of the people, but even the sacred and dignified lamas have gradually lost their faith. Youth, except for a portion coming to Beijing and Beiping for study, mostly study in India and London in Tibet, in Turkey and the Soviet Union in Xinjiang, and in Inner Mongolia many youths flee to Outer Mongolia. Due to their different educations, their views differ greatly upon their return. This is truly a concern for national defense. In the future, reforming the old forces and guiding the new forces will be the core of the Central Government's governance of the frontier. Border defense requires stationing troops and building fortifications, but it is impossible to have a sound social organization without integrating the local people with the people of the interior, eliminating racial and regional prejudice, and fostering a sense of shared hatred towards the enemy, even elite troops will be useless. Furthermore, people in the border areas are prone to suspicion, so those managing border affairs should possess firm perseverance and great magnanimity, avoiding greed for quick gains and short-sightedness, and focusing on the country's long-term plan. Advancing in this way, one will inevitably face slander in one's lifetime, but one's achievements will be seen after death. This is what Qingyang offers to all comrades. (Central News Agency dispatch, 15th)

Liu Wenhui's Troops Attack Deng Jun's Defenses 48

Tian Songyao's Mediation Fails

(Chengdu) On the 12th, 13th, and 14th, Liu Wenhui's army launched a large-scale offensive in four directions against Deng Jun's troops stationed in Pixian, Fanxian, Xinxian, and Zizhong counties. Deng's forces, left with no options, reportedly made contact. Tian Songyao's mediation has failed, and he intends to join the conflict entirely. It is reported that Yang Sen, Li Jiaoyu, and the Chongqing government have all expressed support for Deng. (Special dispatch, 15th)

(Hankou) Liu Wenhui's representative Zhang Boyan, Deng Xihou's representative Wang Xiuyun, Tian Songyao's representative Long Jie, and Yang Sen's representative Zhu Lianyuan traveled together by the "Jihe" steamer to Jiangxi to meet with Chiang Kai-shek to discuss solutions for the Sichuan situation and to visit the front lines of the bandit suppression campaign. Liu Xiang's representative Fu Zhenwu had already gone to Jiangxi. (Special dispatch, 15th)

(Nanjing) Deng Xihou telegraphed Wang Jingwei and Chiang Kai-shek on the 13th, stating that Liu Wenhui sent personnel on the morning of the 6th to attack the garrisoned troops of his command. On the 6th, they occupied Wenjiang County, and on the 9th, they completely seized all of Deng's agencies in Chengdu. Xihou, considering the severity of the national crisis and the fact that the remaining bandits in Sichuan still need to be suppressed, has strived to avoid conflict and retreat step by step. He telegraphed the Central Government on the 6th and 11th. He urged the Central Government to quickly resolve the matter. (Special dispatch, 15th)

Jiang Kai-shek's Instructions at Jiangxi Provincial Party Headquarters Memorial Week 51

The fighting is extremely fierce. He asked how the entire country should rouse itself to jointly face the national crisis, especially as Jiangxi is still in the midst of intense communist suppression efforts. The support work should be done with utmost effort. The bandits have only six counties left, with an estimated fifty thousand people in each county, for a total of no more than three hundred thousand. After years of casualties and desertion, the remaining bandits number less than sixty thousand. Suppressing the communists is not a problem. It should be understood that suppressing the communists is an organizational and total war, with military force accounting for one-third and politics accounting for two-thirds. He hoped that all sectors would work hard and quickly overcome the national crisis and eliminate the communist bandits. (Special dispatch, 15th)

Germany's Relations with England, Austria, and Hungary 84

Papen Refutes British War Secretary's Remarks, Will Lodge Strong Protest with Austria, and Has Tariff Conflict with Hungary

Reuters, Berlin, 14th - Former German Prime Minister and current Deputy Prime Minister Papen gave a speech today at a joint demonstration held by representatives of the National Socialist Party and the Steel Helmet League in Meins, refuting the recent remarks made by British War Secretary Hailsham in the House of Lords. He said that it was outrageous for the War Secretary of a country to issue words about punishment. They personally congratulated him in Lausanne, believing that the delusion that military sanctions could force payment has already died. Now the War Secretary wants to impose sanctions in the League of Nations on a country that is only fighting against immoral treaties, while the League of Nations has taken no action against countries that resort to force and wage war. What hypocrisy! The War Secretary obviously does not know this. He, who still yearns for the political system of the French Revolution, does not know that the new Germany is actually opposed to the escapist's struggles, and should not be regarded as a desire to lean towards war. The escapist's writing wants to highlight the doctrine that those who die on the battlefield do not deserve their death. It should be known that a man's duty to go to the battlefield is like a woman's duty to be a mother. To gain eternal enjoyment, individual sacrifices are indispensable.

Reuters, Vienna, 14th - Germany will lodge a strong diplomatic protest with Austria because the Austrian authorities treated the National Socialist Party delegation led by Dr. Frank with disdain. When the National Socialist Party delegation arrived in Vienna, many people welcomed them, but Austrian officialdom did not welcome their arrival. Austrian Chancellor Dr. Dollfuss spoke strongly, saying that Austria would not accept foreign interference, and the police chief also clearly stated to the National Socialist Party representatives that their visit to Vienna was not genuinely desired by Austrian officialdom.

Havas, Vienna, 14th - Bavarian Minister of Justice Frank, who is visiting Austria, hosted representatives of the foreign press at the German embassy, excluding the French press. Frank declared that the German cabinet ministers had been insulted by the Austrian government upon their arrival in Vienna and would not remain silent. The German government will lodge a protest. Although Frank did not specify the nature of the protest, it is generally speculated that it will involve diplomatic action.

Havas, Vienna, 14th - Prussian Minister of Justice Kerl and other National Socialist Party representatives visiting Austria returned to Germany by plane today. Only Bavarian Minister of Justice Frank remained in Austria. Frank has now departed for the city of Graz in southern Austria.

Havas, Budapest, Hungary, 15th - A tariff conflict between Germany and Hungary is imminent. Germany previously imposed high protectionist taxes on grain, milk, livestock, eggs, vegetables, and fruits imported from Hungary, and is now implementing the same measures on Hungarian oils. This measure would effectively ban all Hungarian exports to Germany. Hungarian sources criticize this move, saying that Germany has granted various benefits to the Netherlands, Belgium, and the Baltic states, while discriminating against Hungary, which violates the most-favored-nation clause. Hungary has dispatched a delegation to Berlin to discuss this matter.

Gandhi's Fasting, Seventh Day, Spirit Still Strong 85

Reuters, Pune, 14th - On the seventh day of Gandhi's fast, he was reunited with his wife and son. Gandhi has not spoken to them for some time due to differences of opinion. It was rumored that Gandhi's health was extremely critical, but according to those who met with him today, although he has not eaten for a week and is weak, his condition is quite good and his spirit is strong. Today, due to the visit of his wife and son, he has rescheduled his usual weekly silence.

American Farmers' Riot 86

Over 20,000 Pounds of Milk Dumped on the Roadside, Police Use Tear Gas to Disperse the Crowd

"National" News, Milwaukee, 14th - Although Farmer Strike Federation Chairman Le Jiao had given an order to indefinitely postpone the strike, today countless farmers waited before dawn on the main roads outside the city, waiting for the milk trucks carrying large quantities of fresh milk from the milk market to come in a steady stream. They immediately held out their canes and intercepted each truck, dumping 25,000 pounds of milk on the roadside. When half of the milk had been dumped, the police arrived and fired tear gas, but because there were few tear gas grenades and many farmers, they were unable to stop them and had to allow the farmers to dump all the milk. When it was all dumped and the large police force had also arrived, the farmers dispersed one after another. Most of them had come in their own cars. It is reported that Rino had sent a telegram to twenty states on Friday, postponing the strike to give the government a chance to implement rural relief. So far, except for Milwaukee, the rest of the places have been able to obey the order.

Anniversary of the Assassination of Prime Minister Inukai, Tokyo Passes Peacefully 87

United News Agency, Tokyo, 15th - At 7:00 PM on this day last year, young military officers and the Farmers' Death Squad assassinated key political figures. Therefore, right-wing groups wanted to take advantage of this opportunity to engage in unruly behavior. Yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, similar leaflets were scattered on the roof garden of the Tokyo Mitsukoshi Department Store. The Metropolitan Police Department received the news and intensified its precautions against right-wing riots. Because of the strict security, everything remained peaceful as of this morning. However, the political and financial circles are indeed very tense. The Seiyukai's movement to overthrow the cabinet seems to have subsided somewhat. It is reported that people like Tokonami and Kuhara have recently distributed statements within their party, saying that the national crisis has not been resolved and the people should not be preoccupied with party strife. The military also criticized the degenerate behavior of party politicians and opposed coups. It is reported that the Japanese government wants to observe the trends in public opinion after the announcement of the May 15th Incident before deciding on its future course.

Page 9

Joint US-British-French Action Seeking a Disarmament Solution to Bring Germany to Compliance, While Other Powers Temporarily Adopt a Defensive Posture 89

A Reuters dispatch from Paris on the 15th: It appears that Britain and France will follow Hitler's lead and issue an important policy statement on Thursday. Reuters learned today from responsible sources that the US representative, Davis, who is familiar with Britain's position, has discussed with French Foreign Minister Poncet the outlines of a joint US-British-French policy. This should not be seen as a plan to jointly resist Germany, as all three countries are now eager to find a way to bring Germany's views closer to those of other nations. However, the overall situation still contains the possibility of danger, so the other powers now have no choice but to adopt a defensive posture.

A National Daily dispatch from Paris on the 14th: US representative to Europe, Davis, returned to Paris last night from London. He expressed the opinion that the disarmament conference has passed its most critical crisis, and there is no immediate danger of it breaking down.

A Reuters dispatch from Geneva on the 14th: Because fourteen countries requested that the disarmament conference postpone the discussions of the General Committee, the chairman of the disarmament conference, Henderson, has postponed the meeting from Monday to Thursday. Because the German representatives returned home to participate in the parliament, the other countries are unwilling to make any responsible statements regarding disarmament before German Chancellor Hitler's speech in the parliament on the 17th of this month. It is heard that the Little Entente countries were the most forceful in requesting the postponement of the meeting.

A National Daily dispatch from Paris on the 15th: Herriot, in his speech at the Radical Socialist Party Congress in Marseille today, recounted his conversations with President Roosevelt during his visit to Washington. He said that the US president firmly insists that the Geneva Disarmament Conference must proceed according to the US disarmament plan. The US president agreed to manage armaments according to the suggestions put forward by France, using methods that are stricter than those stipulated in the British plan. After talking with the president, he knew the dangers that would be caused if Germany were allowed to possess the same types of weapons as other countries. If the disarmament conference shows signs of success, the US president intends to send an observer to the conference to listen to the definition of aggressor nations. If the United States agrees with the decisions made at the conference, then the United States will abandon its long-held neutrality and protect those who are attacked. Mr. Herriot earnestly stated that the US president's attitude on this matter is extremely important, because the League of Nations Covenant Article 16 is thus able to be implemented.

A National Daily dispatch from London on the 15th: Although Britain does not recognize Germany's declaration of its intention to rearm as a violation of the Treaty of Versailles, if Germany's future rearmament plans exceed the limits of the treaty, the British government will consider the sanctions of the Allies to be justified. As for the nature of such sanctions, it is heard that it is currently the objective of diplomatic talks in London and Paris.

A National Daily dispatch from Paris on the 14th: Le Matin published an article today studying the future progress of the disarmament conference, asking what methods would be most practical if it became necessary to implement sanctions. Le Matin's conclusion is that any sanction method is extremely complex. Even implementing Article 430 of the Treaty of Versailles, occupying all or part of the Rhineland area, is no longer a problem, because the implementation of this sanction method is now restricted and weakened by the Hague Conventions. Furthermore, countries that are at risk of being invaded can vigorously implement economic sanctions, but the procedures are also very difficult.

A Havas dispatch from Berlin on the 15th: The German representative to the disarmament conference, Nadolny, arrived in Berlin this morning and went straight to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs.

Washington Closely Watches Progress of Disarmament Conference 90

Roosevelt Intends to Open Difficult Situation, Congress Still Unwilling to Consider Delaying War Debt Payments

US Sends Politicians to Participate in Economic Conference

A Reuters dispatch from Washington on the 14th: Washington authorities are now closely watching the events in Geneva. It is widely believed that the Geneva events will be the key to the debt problem. If the Geneva Disarmament Conference has satisfactory results, then President Roosevelt will definitely take action with Congress before the European countries' debt payments are due in June. If a method of extending and delaying payments is indeed necessary for the success of the disarmament conference, then the US President is prepared to overcome opposition in Congress and request the necessary power to approve the extension of debt payments. However, France opposes repaying the debt due last December that was not paid without obtaining a guarantee of extending and delaying payments. And the US Congress is absolutely unwilling to consider extending the repayment period when the debt is not paid. This is a kind of difficulty encountered by President Roosevelt.

A Reuters dispatch from New York on the 14th reported that the US delegation to the World Economic Conference will have two politicians of established reputation, in order to ensure that political problems do not endanger the future of the World Economic Conference. Secretary of State Hull is satisfied with the current talks in Washington. He hopes that within a period of two months, a general agreement can be reached on common problems.

League of Nations Council Discusses Bolivian-Paraguayan Dispute 91

Paraguayan Representative Argues Declaration of War Did Not Violate Covenant

No Major Battles on Chaco Front

A Havas dispatch from Geneva on the 15th: The Council of the League of Nations met at 10:30 this morning to discuss the dispute between Bolivia and Paraguay. First, the chairman of the Council, Mr. Cerruti of Italy, reported on the process, and then the Bolivian representative, Mr. Reyes, stated that at this time, the Neutral Nations Committee was restarting reconciliation, but Paraguay actually declared war on Bolivia, causing the reconciliation process to be broken. He asked the Council to judge where the final responsibility lies. The Paraguayan representative, Mr. Pedoya, then reviewed the peace proposals put forward by the Paraguayan government on February 25 of this year, Bolivia's reply, and the intervention of the Washington Neutral Nations Committee. He said that Bolivia took every opportunity during the truce of negotiations to increase its military force and attack Paraguay. The Paraguayan representative then read out the notes from the governments of Argentina and Chile to Bolivia. Finally, he said that Paraguay did not initiate the war, and that the war had long existed in fact. Paraguay is now continuing to accept arbitration or legal resolution, and clarified that Paraguay has not violated the clauses of the League of Nations Covenant, so the sanctions of Article 16 of the Covenant cannot be applied.

A National Daily dispatch from the Paraguayan capital on the 14th: A communique from the Paraguayan Ministry of the Army stated that Bolivian troops attempted to carry out an encircling operation in the northern sector of the Chaco front. Their first attempt was repelled by the Paraguayan army. The south and central sectors of the front have not seen much fighting, but there have been signs of aircraft attacks. It is noted that the heat of the sun has slightly decreased and the rainy season has also passed, and the front line can begin a major battle. However, the Bolivian army only has small attacks, which is quite strange. Only because the Bolivian government has threatened to bomb the Paraguayan capital, the people here are still quite panicked.

Egypt Implements New Cotton Tariff 92

A Reuters dispatch from Cairo on the 14th: The Egyptian cabinet meeting approved the revised cotton tariff today as follows: In the future, cotton will be taxed according to the weight per 100 square meters, with different rates. Unbleached cotton weighing 18 kilograms or more per 100 square meters will be taxed at 25 milliemes (Egyptian currency). Bleached cotton will be taxed at 32 milliemes. Colored cotton will be taxed at 40 milliemes. Printed cotton will be taxed at 41 milliemes. All of the above are calculated per net kilogram. Cotton weighing 14 to 18 kilograms will be taxed at 25, 32, 40, and 41 milliemes per net kilogram. Cotton weighing 11 to 14 kilograms will be taxed at 28, 36, 44, and 45 milliemes per net kilogram. Cotton weighing 9 to 10 kilograms will be taxed at 30, 36, 62, and 65 milliemes per net kilogram. Cotton of the same quality weighing 7 to 9 kilograms will be taxed at 30, 36, 65, and 73 milliemes per net kilogram. Cotton weighing 3 to 5 kilograms will be taxed at 35, 50, 100, and 150 milliemes per net kilogram. Cotton weighing less than 3 kilograms per 100 square meters will be taxed at 42, 70, 105, and 160 milliemes per net kilogram.

Japanese Colonial Ministry's Immigration Plan Aims to Completely Colonize Manchuria 93

Jointly Operated Agricultural Development Company by Japan and Manchukuo, Mass Immigration with Capital of 20 Million Yuan, Implementing Group Indoctrination

Tokyo Nichi Nichi Shimbun reported on the 9th that the newly established immigration company, mainly for Manchurian immigrants, recently consulted with the leaders of the Colonial Ministry several times while Lieutenant General Shaoji, Chief of Staff of the Kwantung Army, was staying in Tokyo. The two sides have reached a consensus and decided that Japan and "Manchukuo" will jointly operate the Manchurian Agricultural Development Company with a fixed capital of 20 million yuan. The Colonial Ministry plans to exert the full power of the agricultural land company to massively transfer free agricultural immigrants and develop various industrial immigrants. The Management Bureau will formulate specific plans. The outline is to set 100,000 families, 500,000 people, in units of five-person families, and immigrate within 10 to 15 years. After immigrating to Manchuria, group indoctrination will be implemented under the supervision of the Kwantung Army. New immigrant training centers will be established in four places: Harbin, Fengtian, Gongzhuling, and Xiongyuecheng. The Kwantung Army Special Service Department, the Colonial Ministry, and the Governor-General of Korea, and other immigration-related authorities and technical officials discussed the immigration policy to Manchuria at the Special Service Department Conference Room in Changchun on the 7th, establishing specific plans. First, a joint immigration agricultural land investigation committee will be opened to discuss the problems of controlling and contacting immigrant organizations in Manchuria, the problem of distributing immigrants to Korea, the problem of defending immigrant areas, the establishment and investigation of the Manchurian Agricultural Land Development Company, etc. As a result, specialists will organize an immigrant investigation team, with the Colonial Ministry dispatching two people, and the Governor-General of Korea, the Kwantung Government, the Kwantung Army, Manchuria, and the South Manchuria Railway each dispatching one person to organize the first team, led by engineer Nakamura, to depart from Jilin northward on the 10th with the protection of the Jilin army to investigate. On the 12th, a second team, led by engineer Kato, was organized to depart to the south of Jilin Province. The third team will investigate the Fengtian area from the 20th.

Also, according to the Tokyo Asahi Shimbun, the current president of the South Manchuria Railway, Mr. Hatta, is currently secretly plotting with various parties in the Japanese government in Tokyo to carry out the immigration business to our four eastern provinces in order to achieve the complete colonization of Manchuria. Recently, Hatta has concluded discussions with the Colonial Ministry authorities on this issue and will meet with all parties to further discuss specific implementation plans. The main content of his plan is to organize a Manchurian Agricultural Land Development Company and set up an investment agency with capital of 30 million to 40 million yuan. The company will use 20 million yuan of capital to purchase farmland in Manchuria to await the free immigration of Japanese people. A system of self-cultivating farmers will be created through the fifteen-year installment method, requiring the accommodation of a total of 200,000 families, with an agricultural immigrant population of one million. The plan will be included in the Colonial Ministry's new business in next year's budget. The newspaper also reported that the Colonial Ministry's second armed immigrant trip to Manchuria has already selected 700 qualified people from 18 prefectures and counties throughout Japan, including Tohoku, Hokuriku, Chubu, and Kanto. Another exam will be given on the 15th of this month, and 500 people will be selected to be transferred to the army factory in Gunma Prefecture to implement emergency military training. It is scheduled to depart for Manchuria in early July. The Japanese call them the avant-garde immigrants.

— Reached

Fierce Bloodshed at Nantianmen for Days, Heavy Casualties on Both Sides, Enemy Troops East of Luan River Have Crossed River to Invade West, Intense Fighting

Enemy Planes Bomb Everywhere, Disrupting Our Rear

A special dispatch from Peiping: The Japanese army is actively plotting to disrupt Tianjin and Peiping, scheming to shake our northern military base to achieve the first step of their dream of aggression, planning to occupy Miyun in the north and invade Luanzhou in the east, seizing the important areas around Tianjin and Peiping, and then using political methods to use traitors to launch riots in Tianjin and Peiping, responding from within and without, in one fell swoop to compensate for their long-cherished wish. Since the enemy east of the Luan River occupied our Qian'an, Lulong, Funing, and Changli counties, there has been no active action on the railway front. They are purely using the method of flanking attacks, crossing the river upstream of the Luan River to invade the west, avoiding fighting along the Beining line to avoid causing international attention. Since the 11th, the Japanese puppet troops in Qian'an and Lulong have begun to advance into our Luanxi, using artillery, airplanes, and smoke bombs as cover to forcibly cross the river. Another route built a bridge at night from the Xixiakou northwest of Lulong to cross the river. Our Wang Yizhe's troops, and He (Lizhong) and Weng (Zhaoyuan)'s divisions did their best to resist. Gunfire was clearly heard in Leizhuang and Guye. At 2:00 p.m., Weng Zhaoyuan personally led reinforcements to repel the enemy.

This morning, fierce battles took place in Sunluozhuang and Wang Guanying, which are 60 miles away from Shaheyi. The enemy troops planned to divide into two routes to raid Luanzhou. This morning, our army sent a large number of reinforcements to block. As of press time, the battle is still going on. The situation in that area is extremely critical. Fortunately, our certain division's left flank was harassed and attacked by the enemy, and we sent powerful troops to defend it early. They are all in a bitter battle. I heard Yu Yizhe's article (12th) at noon.

On the Gubeikou side, since our army abandoned the Nantianmen position, the front line is at Daxiao Xinkailing, the right flank is at Daohuangyu, and the left flank is at Shangdianzi. The enemy army launched a general offensive on the 10th, dividing into routes from Nantianmen and Heilongtan to bombard our position with artillery and airplanes, followed by infantry charges. The fierce battle has been going on for days, with more than 2,000 casualties on both sides. Our Liu division suffered heavy losses, and one part was transferred back for reorganization, and another army was transferred to resist. The battle has been fierce day and night for the past two days, and has not stopped until last night. Last night, our left and right flank positions changed slightly, and the front also withdrew to Xiaoxinkailing, Beixiangyu and other places. Since our army abandoned the Nantianmen position, there are more passes in the mountains and the front line is too long, making defense more difficult. Brother Strangled to Death for Land 99

The incident occurred in No. 596, Beitou Lane, in the Second District (Jingyun City), only five or six miles from the city. There is a villager named Bao Shunsheng in the lane, whose wife Deng gave birth to three sons. The eldest and second sons are already married, but Rong Fa is not yet married. The three brothers divided the property in 1921. On the 11th of this month, Rong Fa had nothing to do and was suffering from sores, so he returned to his hometown to live. On the evening of the 12th, Rong Fa planned to borrow 10 yuan from Jin Fa, but Jin Fa refused. Rong Fa then demanded the return of the land deed he had lent to him before, which caused a dispute. Jin Fa became angry and punched Rong Fa. Rong Fa saw that the situation was not good and ran away. The matter subsided. Unexpectedly, at about 11:00 p.m. on the (13th) night before, Rong Fa had fallen asleep when Jin Fa suddenly sneaked into his residence, put a hemp rope around Rong Fa's neck, and strangled him hard. Rong Fa woke up and shouted for help. Jin Fa then struck his head several times with a long bench, killing him on the spot.

After offsetting the income and expenses, there is still a surplus. The county government will announce a tender for demolition soon.

Page 10

Local News

Expiration of the Sino-Japanese Tariff Agreement

New Taxes and Surcharges to Be Levied from Today 110

Significant Differences Between Using Customs Gold Units for Calculation, Surcharges Previously Exempted Now All Levied

The Sino-Japanese Tariff Agreement expired yesterday (May 15th). Starting today, all imported Japanese goods will be subject to the new tariff and two additional surcharges. Yesterday, the Jianghai Customs authorities received an order from the Ministry of Finance to implement the new tariff based on customs gold units and issued a notice to levy the surcharges starting today. Details are as follows:

Levy of New Taxes 111

The collection of new taxes begins upon the expiration of the agreement. The difference between the tariff rates promulgated on January 1st, 1931, and those maintained by the Sino-Japanese Reciprocal Agreement is significant. Furthermore, the old agreement was calculated in silver during its effective period, while our customs have long used customs gold units for tax collection. Japanese goods have uniquely benefited from silver-based calculations, with substantial profits. At the current silver price of $1.40 per yuan, the customs gold unit requires nearly two yuan. The difference in payment significantly differs. The change to collecting new taxes in customs gold units results in a difference of about double the benefits enjoyed under the tariff agreement.

Levy of Surcharges 112

The Ministry of Finance previously ordered all customs offices to levy customs surcharges and disaster relief surcharges on imported and exported goods. Imported and exported goods from all countries were subject to these surcharges. However, the Sino-Japanese Tariff Agreement stipulated in Article 3 that various surcharges were to be exempted. Therefore, Japanese goods have been able to avoid paying these surcharges in recent years. With the expiration of the agreement, this exemption naturally becomes invalid, and starting today, all surcharges will be levied on Japanese goods in accordance with the regulations.

Order from the Ministry of Finance 113

The Jianghai Customs Supervisory Office received an instruction from the Ministry of Finance, stating that, in order to implement the matter, the surcharges collected by customs were originally stipulated to be levied on import and export taxes. When the surcharges were implemented in December 1931, the attached schedule to the Sino-Japanese Agreement was still in effect. Therefore, based on Article 3 of the original regulations, various items were exempted from surcharges. However, as the attached schedule to the Sino-Japanese Agreement expired on May 15th of this year, the basis for the aforementioned exemptions no longer exists. Starting May 16th, these imported goods should be subject to surcharges to ensure uniformity. The matter has been submitted to the Executive Yuan for record, and the Customs Administration has been ordered to handle it accordingly.

Customs Notice 114

We earnestly request that your association telegraph the central government and the authorities of various provinces to quickly dispatch aircraft to the front to defend against the enemy and boost our military morale. Huang Shouzhong, Commander of the First Army of the Rehe People's Anti-Japanese National Salvation Army; Zhou Han, Commander of the Independent Seventh Detachment of the First Army Corps of the Northeast Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army."

French Community Celebrates Joan of Arc Day 120

France Still Commemorates the Patriotic Heroine Who Saved the Country 500 Years Ago

The day before yesterday was the French Joan of Arc Day, commemorating the French maiden who dedicated herself to saving the country. The French community in this city held a grand celebration. The origin of Joan of Arc Day dates back approximately 503 years ago. Most of France was occupied by British troops, and the country's situation was critical and its morale was low. The urgent situation was no less severe than our country's situation today. In the southern region of France, there was a small town called Orleans, which had been besieged for a long time. The soldiers in the town were exhausted. Just as it was about to fall, a maiden named Joan knew her duty as a woman and mourned the sinking of her country. Relying on her religious beliefs, she gathered soldiers, inspired them with loyalty and righteousness, encouraged them with divine destiny, dispelled their fear of the enemy and desire for temporary peace, and led more than 5,000 people with incomplete weapons to fight and win. The British army lifted the siege of Orleans. From then on, the French soldiers were determined to fight, their morale was greatly boosted, and they won consecutive battles, recovering most of the lost land. Unfortunately, Joan was deceived by traitors, captured by the British army, falsely accused of being a witch, burned at the stake, and martyred. However, from then on, France was finally able to reverse the declining trend and establish the foundation for its revival. The French people remembered her heroic deeds and designated the day of her martyrdom as a national memorial day, which is observed as solemnly as the Democratic Memorial Day on July 14th. At 9 AM the day before yesterday, the French Consul General Mei Liai, accompanied by the commander of the navy and army and representatives of the French community, held a flag-raising ceremony at the consulate square. Then, at around 10 AM, they went to the Catholic Church in Yangjingbang to hold a grand mass to commemorate this patriotic heroine with an extremely solemn ceremony.

Using Foreign Backgrounds to Fulfill Their Ambitions, a Free City as Its Ultimate Goal

According to China United News Agency in this city, our agency received a telegram from Tokyo last night, stating that the Japanese in Shanghai have organized a Foreign Residents' Association to use the backgrounds of foreign residents in Shanghai to echo the Japanese army in North China and re-raise the issue of a free city in order to fulfill their ambitions over the years. This group is to be the backing for the so-called free city plan. Yesterday, the organization's declaration, which consisted of 15 articles, was released. The main points are excerpted as follows: (1) The purpose is to maintain unity and cooperation among foreigners in Shanghai and promote the peace, security, and prosperity of this metropolis. Since last year, several foreigners have often met to discuss various issues that are closely related to the interests of the foreign community. (2) The opinions of the comrades have reached a consensus that there is no other way to effectively express the opinions of the foreign residents' organizations, chambers of commerce, and foreign residents in Shanghai except to organize this association. (3) According to the existing laws of the Public Concession, only 30% of the foreign residents have the right to vote. The remaining 70% have no opportunity to express their opinions on issues that are closely related to their interests. (4) The primary purpose of this association is to protect the interests of foreign residents in various countries. Any foreign resident residing in Shanghai who is over 18 years old can become a member of this association by paying an annual membership fee of only one yuan. (5) We often hear foreign residents say that there are issues that are deeply related to our interests but have no opportunity for consultation because there was no proper organization in the past. (6) The most important research topics of this association should be the interests of foreign residents in all parts of China and Shanghai, especially the administrative facilities of Shanghai and the promotion of peace, security, and prosperity. (7) The advantage of this association is that it can maintain close contact with existing organizations in various countries. When a certain organization in a certain country wants to request its government to take necessary actions for the benefit of its foreign residents, this association will be the backing to connect various organizations to assist in the implementation of its ambitions. (8) In order to ensure that the interests of Shanghai citizens are consistent, this association wants to work closely with the Chinese Taxpayers Association and other industrial and commercial organizations. (9) This association can submit opinions on issues related to the interests of foreign residents in Shanghai to the diplomatic corps, consular corps, and the League of Nations. Although no certain issues have occurred at present, they will always occur in the future. (10) Regardless of whether it is a local issue or an issue of general interest to foreign residents, it should not be considered from the sole position of one country. We should assess and study countermeasures from the perspective of the overall interests of foreign residents in Shanghai. Only by maintaining this principle can we maintain the common interests of foreign residents. (11) The temporary committee of this association will be initially nominated by organizations and chambers of commerce in various countries. (12) The current temporary committee will continue to perform its duties during this year. After the articles of association are drafted at the end of this year, the members will be asked for their consent. (13) The strength of this association depends entirely on the members and foreign residents in Shanghai. (14) The committee members of this association deeply believe that strength should come from unity. Therefore, we sincerely hope that foreign residents will provide strong assistance. (15) We hope that everyone who receives this letter will fill in their names on the membership certificate and send it along with the membership fee of one yuan to help the activities of this association. All donations are welcome. It is heard that the Japanese Civic Group will force all Japanese residents to join in order to manipulate the actual power. Another Japanese organization has been added to Shanghai.

International Labour Conference to Discuss Reduction of Working Hours 130

Preparatory Meeting Has Produced Draft Agreement Aims to Achieve a Forty-Hour Work Week

The Central News Agency reports that the International Labour Office broadcast the key agenda items of the upcoming 17th Labour Conference from 8:00 PM to 12:00 AM the day before yesterday via the Geneva radio station. Our local Transportation Ministry's International Radio Station monitored the broadcast, and our agency has translated the key points as follows:

The 17th International Labour Conference, hosted by the International Labour Office, is scheduled to open in Geneva on June 8th. The fifth item on its agenda is to consider the report on the reduction of working hours submitted by the preparatory meeting. The preparatory meeting was held in Geneva in January of this year, with representatives from 35 countries participating. The U.S. Consul in Geneva also attended as an observer, acting on instructions from Washington. The meeting conducted preliminary research on the reduction of working hours as a means to alleviate worldwide unemployment, with particular attention to the forty-hour work week plan. After the meeting, a report was drafted and sent to various governments on February 14th, requesting that they submit their opinions before April 15th. The Labour Office then compiled these opinions and drafted a grey-blue report for discussion at the conference. The report includes a draft agreement on the reduction of working hours, stipulating that the working hours of industrial, factory, mining, commercial, and other factory workers should be reduced by up to three hours per week compared to the maximum working hours stipulated in previous agreements, thus covering a wide range. Almost all workers are included except for agricultural and water transport workers. However, due to the different circumstances of various workers, it seems necessary to draft three types of agreement for selection. In general, the conference will first pass two types of agreement, with the third type only for discussion and the decision on whether to adopt it will be made at the next meeting. The draft regarding factory workers is largely based on the Washington Agreement, with an average of forty hours per week. The definition of "working hours" in the draft remains the same as in the 1930 agreement, namely the time during which employed workers are subject to the employer's direction. Detailed provisions are also included for the calculation of average working hours, with particular attention to methods of reducing working hours, employing new workers, and facilitating management. For work with special circumstances, special regulations are made for working hours and shift arrangements. However, in the event of unexpected or emergency situations, the limits on working hours may be temporarily lifted. The principle for limiting coal mine working hours is 40 hours per week, with the general provisions being the same as the 1931 agreement, namely a maximum of seven hours and forty-five minutes for daily underground work, and an average of thirty-eight hours and forty-five minutes per week, excluding Sundays and holidays. Several clauses of the three draft agreements are completely identical, such as the special provisions in the event of special emergencies. In summary, although the purpose of these agreements is to alleviate unemployment, they are independent of previous agreements and do not modify them. These agreements are temporary rather than permanent in nature. The draft also stipulates that the agreement will come into effect three months after ratification, but the duration of the agreement has not been specified, pending a decision by the conference.

Commodity Inspection Bureau Writes to Chamber of Commerce to Explain Commodity Inspection Authority 133

The Commodity Inspection Bureau yesterday wrote to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce to explain its commodity inspection authority. The original letter stated: Greetings. We received your letter Shang Zi No. 306, which stated that the Intestine Industry Association had reported that members of the China Intestine Factory had complained that recently, meat inspectors from the Municipal Health Bureau had stopped shipments of pig intestines, forcing them to pay inspection fees according to the regulations for inspecting cured hams, but pig intestines have always been inspected by the Commodity Inspection Bureau. Therefore, they requested that you forward their request to the Municipal Health Bureau to instruct the meat inspectors to exempt pig intestines from inspection and fees. We are therefore writing to your bureau to request that you forward our request to the Health Bureau to stop duplicate inspections of pig intestines in order to comply with statutory authority and avoid extra burdens on intestine merchants. In response, Article 1 of the Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau's regulations for inspecting meat entering the city stipulates that the bureau shall notify our bureau to send personnel to inspect meat products sold abroad. Therefore, sausage casings manufactured in Shanghai and shipped abroad after inspection by our bureau are no longer inspected by the Health Bureau. However, whether pig intestines should be inspected when entering the city is within the authority of the Health Bureau. Please write directly to the Health Bureau to discuss this matter. We are writing to inform you for your information.

According to the National News Agency, China National Aviation Corporation has completed the entire Shanghai-Chengdu line and is adding Shanghai-Guangdong and Sichuan-Guizhou routes, as well as related news about the Haizhou, Nantong, and Qingdao airports. Secretary Li of the company gave reporters a detailed account yesterday, which is recorded below:

Confirmed Date for Trial Flight on Chongqing-Chengdu Route 137

After the company sent personnel to negotiate with the authorities in Sichuan on flying the Chongqing-Chengdu section, active preparations began. It was originally scheduled for a trial flight yesterday. Now, because the aircraft to be used for the trial flight has been decided to be the No. 12 Stinson land plane, it needs to be refitted with a specially made thick glass fuselage. Other radio materials also need to be purchased for installation on the plane in Chengdu. Therefore, the date has been delayed. It is now decided that the trial flight will take place on June 1st. If the results are good, the official opening will take place the next day without further delay.

Additional Shanghai-Guangdong and Sichuan-Guizhou Routes 138

Preparing the Shanghai-Guangdong route was originally a planned project of the company. However, the report from Hong Kong stating that the opening was scheduled for July 1st is not accurate. The company is currently actively completing the Chongqing-Chengdu section of the Shanghai-Chengdu line. Once that section is officially opened, the Shanghai-Guangdong air route will be implemented. The route will go from Shanghai via Wenzhou, Xiamen, etc., to Guangzhou or extend to Hong Kong. This section can use seaplanes and is easier to prepare. It can be realized around mid-August. The Sichuan-Guizhou route is from Chengdu to Guiyang, and the route passes through high mountains and ridges, making flying more difficult. It will generally be organized after the Shanghai-Guangdong route is completed.

Haizhou, Nantong, and Qingdao Airports 139

The Haizhou Airport on the company's Shanghai-Ping lines has completed the construction of station houses and gas stations. In Nantong, in order to prevent bad weather, it is planned to set up a reserve airport using civilian land, which has been approved by the Ministry of Transportation. Technical Assistant Yu Shipu has been sent to Tong to work with the county government. The electric poles and jetties around the Qingdao Airport that previously obstructed flight have been requested to be moved by the Qingdao Municipal Government and the Telephone Bureau, and they have agreed to implement this.

Ancient Tree Struck by Lightning 148

Yesterday (May 15th), the weather was hot. Around 3:00 PM in the afternoon, dark clouds gathered and lightning flashed. A heavy rain poured down, and thunder rumbled. An ancient tree, over ten feet tall, in the Qitaitou area of Meizhou Road, Yangshupu, Shanghai East, was suddenly struck in two pieces during the thunderstorm. It was not until after 4:00 PM, when the rain stopped and the sky cleared, that the nearby residents discovered it. For a time, people gathered from far and wide to watch, almost like a human mountain. Someone suggested that there must be something strange about the tree being struck, and claimed that the wood from the struck tree could cure diseases. As a result, in an instant, the remaining wood of the tree was seized and emptied by the onlookers.

Extortion Letters Belong to the Party Involved In Publishing An Advertisement To Express Sincerity 151

Those belonging to the category used money to put the telegram in the pole letterbox to inquire on behalf of the party concerned as agreed

The Extortionist And His Second Landlord Were Arrested

Zhu Panquan, a native of Suzhou, lives at No. 2, Lane 201, Tongfu Road. Last year, during the January 28th incident in Shanghai, he suddenly received a threatening letter from someone claiming to be Huang Hua, with rather激烈 words, hoping to extort 5,000 yuan. If he agreed to pay, Zhu was instructed to publish a reply in the newspaper. After receiving the letter, Zhu reported the information to the Jing'an Temple Police Station because he was running a light business and had economic difficulties. On the one hand, he published a reply in the newspaper. On February 13th of last year, he received another letter asking to contact him near the Great World on February 12th. Because the date had passed, it was not implemented. Unexpectedly, on May 2nd and 8th of this year, he received two letters in succession, and the amount of the request was changed to 1,000 yuan. If he agreed, he still had to publish an advertisement on the cover of the Xinwen Bao to express his sincerity. Zhu then acted according to the letter. On the 11th, he received a reply from Huang Hua, asking him to prepare the money and send it to the paper letterbox on the telegraph pole at the entrance of Songqing Lane, No. 80, Daokou Chong Alley, Zhuanwan, Jingtu Street, Xicang Street in the city at 11:00 PM on the 12th. A paper with the name Huang Hua seeking people was posted on the telegraph pole. If the money was placed properly, the paper bearing the name Huang Hua could be torn in half as a sign. Zhu immediately reported to the police station and ordered Detective Fan Defu, Detective Jin Yangwu, and other detectives from the Public Security Bureau to disguise themselves and go to the place to ambush. On one side, a representative, Zhu Yongquan, was sent to take the prepared newspaper in the style of banknotes and put it into the paper letterbox. Soon, Qian Hongsheng, a local man living at No. 10, Yixing Lane, Daokou Chong Alley, came slowly and put his hand into the paper letterbox to take out the paper package when he was arrested by the detectives. A rifle and 50 bullets were seized at his home, and Qian confessed without denying it. However, the detectives also seized the items used to write the letter, which were provided by the second landlord, Xu Haokun, and brought them into the Public Security Bureau on the 13th, returning to the police station. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the Criminal Court of the First Special District Local Court for interrogation by Judge Wu Tingqi. The police station's lawyer, Li Zhishan, accused them of violating Article 2 of the Punishment of Bandits Ordinance and Article 370 of the Criminal Law, and said that the handwriting of the defendant still needs to be identified, so the five threatening letters cannot be presented as evidence and requested a postponement. Then Detective Fan reported the situation of the arrest. The plaintiff, Zhu Panquan, went to Su for important matters and entrusted his relative Wu Chengliang to represent him in court to explain the facts of the case. Zhu Yongquan also testified to prove everything. When asked, the defendant confessed that it was because of the impact of the January 28th incident, his family was destroyed, and because he was unemployed and had no foothold, he took this course of action. This matter was done by him alone and there were no accomplices. When Xu Haokun was questioned, he denied the charges. Judge Wu instructed that the case be rescheduled for further interrogation.

A Scene from the Annual Shooting Competition of the Shanghai Volunteer Corps 154

Chinese Team Wins the Entire Corps Machine Gun Cup with Three Victories

The annual national shooting competition of the Shanghai Volunteer Corps is held every year to see the shooting results of each team. The competition period this year is from May 6th to 21st. Competitions are held on Saturdays and Sundays, and the number of contestants who have signed up is extremely enthusiastic. The types of competitions are also more numerous than in previous years.

機關槍杯縮影 155

The competition was most intense in the Machine Gun Cup. It is known that last Sunday (the 14th) was the day dedicated to the machine gun competition. On that day, players from various countries gathered at the shooting range to compete for victory. A total of twenty-two teams participated, each with four players. The course was an offensive type. The players were pre-positioned at the 500-yard mark. Upon seeing the target rise, they immediately carried their guns and sprinted forward to the 400-yard mark, where they fired forty shots in rapid succession. Then, they advanced to the 300-yard mark and fired another forty shots. The time limit from start to finish was two minutes. The Chinese team's second squad won, scoring 138 points, ranking first among the machine gun teams from various countries. As usual, they won the National Machine Gun Cup (the cup was a gift from the former Chairman of the Municipal Council, Mr. Rawlings, and is quite tall). The players were Ye Renqian, Ni Ruilong, Zhang Songyuan, and Wu Huaqi. Second place went to the Shanghai Light Artillery Team, with 117 points. Third place also went to the Chinese team, the sixteenth squad, with 105 points. The Chinese team has always been renowned for machine gun shooting, and this victory marks their third time winning, truly deserving of praise.

漕河涇監獄參觀記 162

A Visit to the Caohejing Prison 163

Lawyer Dong Kang submitted a petition to the Ministry of Justice on behalf of the prisoners on the 12th of this month, requesting a thorough investigation of the Jiangsu Second Model Prison in Caohejing for deducting food rations and mistreating prisoners. The Ministry of Justice has not yet made a formal response to the case. The content is of concern to advocates of humanity. A reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency drove to Caohejing yesterday to investigate the situation. The details are not exhaustive in a glimpse. The following is a record of the visit:

The Warden's Attitude: When the reporter arrived at the Second Prison, he immediately met with Warden Tian Jinghua. According to him, he believed that there was no need to defend himself against lawyer Dong Kang's petition, and he welcomed all sectors and the press to investigate and visit at any time to prove the truth. Moreover, the Director and Section Chief of the Prison Department of the Ministry of Justice and the Section Chief of the High Court regularly inspected the prison, so the competent authorities also attached great importance to the lives of criminals in the prison.

Number of Inmates: He continued that there were more than 1,700 inmates in the prison, with criminal offenders accounting for more than 1,600, political prisoners accounting for more than 120, and two Western offenders. There were more than 1,500 male inmates and more than 180 female inmates. Among the female inmates, most were opium offenders.

Distribution of All Prison Cells: These more than 1,700 criminals, apart from the female prisoners who are housed in more than 40 separate cells, the rest are housed in 264 cells, divided into seven types: A, B, C, D, E, F, and G. The 60 G-type cells originally housed one person each, but due to overcrowding, they have been changed to house three people each. The remaining six types house a maximum of 14 people, with an average of 11 or 12 people.

Expenditure of 8,000 Yuan: The prison's monthly expenditure is allocated by the Military and Political Department and the Finance Department of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, totaling 8,000 yuan, including expenses for prisoner rations, clothing, medicine, and construction. Criminal prisoners' rations are one dime, and political prisoners' rations are one dime and five cents, with the remainder used for clothing, medicine, hygiene, and other expenses. However, there is always a slight surplus each month for expansion and subsidies. Up to now, the surplus totals 2,400 yuan, which is deposited in the prison for emergencies and the accounts are submitted to the Supreme Court for review.

Ration Supply is Ample: The actual need for one dime's worth of rations for criminal offenders and one dime and five cents' worth of rations for political prisoners is between 8.5 or 9 cents, with an average surplus of 1.5 cents. However, political prisoners receive better treatment than criminal offenders. For example, the price of tea provided is higher than that for criminal offenders. If we only talk about rations, the two sides actually come from the same pot and there is not much difference. The rice eaten by the prisoners is small-milled rice, and the side dishes are vegetables, taro, and beans.

Attention to Prisoner Hygiene: There were originally only two doctors in terms of hygiene. Since I took office in December last year, I have added a third. They are indeed extremely busy treating prisoners every day. Haircuts and shaves are held once a week. There is a bathhouse that can accommodate 20 people each time. Due to limited funds, the pool is small and there are many people, so they have to take turns every day. I have now submitted a request to the Ministry of Justice to expand the original bathhouse, hoping that it can accommodate 100 people each time, so that the nearly 2,000 prisoners can all bathe a dozen times a day.

Denial of Confiscation of Sent Items: As for the confiscation of prisoner items and work products, there is evidence to check and I can absolutely take responsibility. When family members send items, in addition to the prison issuing a formal receipt, the prisoners themselves also add their fingerprints. It is definitely not possible to confiscate them arbitrarily. In the future, it may be possible to ask the prisoners' families to review them.

Ordinary Prisoners Can Communicate: Stopping communication and withholding mail is based on the law. It is because political prisoners may have other destructive and propaganda actions, so this restriction only applies to political prisoners, not ordinary criminal prisoners. As for saying that lawyer Dong Kang's two prisoners, only Lu Zongduan is indeed in prison. There is no such person as Wang Jiaxiang. Lu Zongduan is one of the political prisoners. He was recently sent to Xin Puyu Hall for medical treatment due to illness. His accusation may have arisen at this time.

Lu Zongduan's Own Account: Afterwards, the warden brought Lu Zongduan to meet with the reporter. According to Lu's own account, he completely denied lawyer Dong Kang's petition to the Ministry of Justice and said that he was 31 years old, a native of Hubei. He was originally an editor at the Hubei Minbao newspaper. He was arrested in Shanghai in February of the 20th year of the Republic of China for a Communist Party case and sentenced to ten years in prison. He was given a three-year reduction in sentence during the amnesty. The treatment in prison is still good and he can eat his fill every meal. However, he denied going to Xin Puyu Hall for medical treatment. At that time, Lu was wearing a blue-gray short shirt and trousers with a black padded jacket. He was healthy and not in a state of despair.

Complete Inspection Once: After the warden's oral account, he guided the reporter to visit all the prisons at the reporter's request. The interior cleaning was still clean, but the air was not very circulating and the stench was unbearable. Although the rice cooked in the kitchen was rough, it was still edible. However, the side dishes cooked seemed not very well done and were half-cooked. The prison has various small handicrafts such as spinning, weaving, knitting, printing, typesetting, toothbrush making, and pasting paper boxes. The funds total 3,000 yuan. More than 1,100 people are working, and those who are not working are either political prisoners who want to engage in propaganda or are sick. The profit distribution is about one-quarter to one-fifth per prisoner, and each prisoner can get about 1.5 to 2 dimes a day. Inside the prison, apart from working hours, they get up at 6 am every morning, start working at 7:30 am, and go to sleep at 9 pm.

鄞縣四貨展覽會延期 164

Yinxian National Products Exhibition Postponed 165

A Meeting Was Held by Participating Factories Yesterday

The Shanghai Citizens' National Products Promotion Association and the China National Products Maintenance Association, as the Yinxian National Products Exhibition Preparatory Committee, decided to postpone the opening to the 15th of next month because the free transportation reduction forms have not yet been issued and the construction of the venue has not been completed in time. It is reported that the entire plan, in particular, convened the Third Factory Representatives' Conference at the Association Hall in Jiumudi at 3 pm yesterday. Representatives from Xianshi Cosmetics Factory, Limin Dyeing and Weaving Factory, Zhenhua Manufacturing Factory, Yabu Er Electric Appliance Factory, etc., totaling 118 people, were publicly elected Chen Yiting as the chairman, and the ceremony was performed as usual. First, the chairman reported on the purpose of the meeting, stating that the association, in order to expand the national products movement and awaken the people in the interior, gather the power of national products to save the country, led the factories to participate in the Yinxian National Products Exhibition and sent personnel to Ningbo to repeatedly negotiate with the local presiding authorities and reach a compromise. The opening was scheduled for the 20th of this month, and all factories participated enthusiastically and actively prepared all the procedures that have been completed. Now that the General Assembly has resolved to postpone the opening to June 15, the future of the association is extremely important. In the end, the chairman summarized the opinions of the group and resolved as follows: (1) Send a letter to the General Assembly requesting the opening to be advanced to June 1; (2) Publicly elect Zhu representative Haichao to go to Ningbo again to firmly request; (3) The Dinghai National Products Exhibition will be held in connection after the closing of the Ningbo Exhibition, with a term of only one week to preserve the original plan of other national products exhibitions; (4) Committee member Zheng Liankun will still be responsible for the construction of the venue; (5) Prepare oil tarpaulins and generators and allocate funds from the association's fund to the executive committee for quick handling.
