公共租界四月份衛生狀况 170

Sanitary Conditions in the International Settlement in April 171

The report of the Commissioner of Public Health for April states that the death rate for foreigners this month was 13.10 per thousand, compared to 15.45 last month. The main reason for the decrease was the reduction in deaths from pneumonia. The death rate for Chinese this month was 10.30, compared to 130.6 last month. This report is not complete, but it is enough to show that the public health has improved. In terms of birth statistics, 39 births were reported for foreigners and 123 births were recorded for Chinese. Regarding the method of statistics, the Department of Statistics of the Lister Institute of Medical Research and experts from the London School of Hygiene in Shanghai have been asked to review it in order to improve it.

The infectious diseases prevalent among foreigners are scarlet fever, diphtheria, and tuberculosis, but scarlet fever has shown a decreasing trend. This is also due to seasonal factors. Among the Chinese, smallpox, tuberculosis, and cerebrospinal meningitis are more common. Cerebrospinal meningitis is also trending downwards. The discovery of mad dogs has increased recently. The public should pay more attention to the supervision of the dogs they keep. The number of vaccinations against smallpox this month was 8,111 handled by the motor vehicle team and 23,691 handled by the various health divisions, totaling 86,748 people vaccinated from the beginning of January to the end of April.

The production of milk this month decreased by 3.5% compared to March. The chemical analysis and microbial tests of milk were generally satisfactory. All A-grade milk met the standards. The work in the slaughterhouses was roughly the same as usual. The price of vegetables in the small vegetable markets did not fluctuate much. The inspections of bakeries day and night were generally satisfactory. The spring cleaning of food stores was carried out according to regulations and the situation was quite improved.

Mosquito eradication work started earlier this year. The first step is to clear the rivers and ditches, and do everything possible to eliminate all places where mosquitoes breed. The water accumulation in the open space opposite the Licha Restaurant has also been started to be removed.

急救時疫醫院診務繁忙 172

The Emergency Epidemic Hospital is Busy with Medical Services 173

The Emergency Epidemic Hospital at the northern end of Beixizang Road and Kaifeng Road was established by Shanghai celebrities Du Yuesheng, Wang Xiaolai, Jin Tingsun, Yao Mulian, Zhang Weirou, Kui Yanfang, Pang Jingzhou, Yang Yusheng, Zhou Bangjun, etc. It is well-equipped and large in scale. The hospital's purpose is to rescue the poor and sick and eliminate epidemics. No fees are charged for medicine, ward, gold, or hospitalization. The hospital cures tens of millions of epidemic cases every year. The outpatient department is also very crowded, treating internal and external medicine, and the number of people seeking medical treatment reaches more than 400 every day. Over the years, the treatment results have been well-received and it is truly a valuable charitable organization in Shanghai. The hospital's expenses rely entirely on the continuous input of enthusiastic people from all walks of life and the efforts of the hospital directors to raise funds. Now that it is the summer season, it will cost even more to accommodate epidemic patients. It is heard that the funds for this year are about to be raised.

拾球人死得慘 182

The Ball Retriever Died Tragically 183

丨Drowned While Entering Xiaohama to Retrieve a Ball丨

Shi Yongqing, a 40-year-old man from Haimen who lived at No. 4, Huanglu Road, Jiangwan Road, is currently working as a shop clerk at the Jinye Exchange on Jiujiang Road with a monthly salary of 21 yuan. However, in addition to his wife, he also has four sons and four daughters, so his life is difficult. Therefore, Shi went to the Japanese Corefu Ball Field in Hongkou Target Field every morning at 9 am to retrieve balls, earning a daily wage of 2 dimes, which he used to supplement his household expenses. Yesterday morning at nearly 9 am, Shi went to the field to retrieve balls as usual. Suddenly, a ball rolled into the opposite Hama. A certain Japanese player ordered Shi Yongqing to enter the water to retrieve the ball. The Hama was about two or three zhang deep. After Shi entered the water, he drowned tragically. Then, someone salvaged the body and sent it to the Tongren Hospital for transfer to the coroner's office for examination.

外國絲綢店有縱火圖賠嫌疑 184

Foreign Silk Store Suspected of Arson for Insurance Money 185

A Lot of Inflammable Materials Were Found in the Store, and the Austrian Manager and Others Were Detained

The Naowu Erde (transliteration) foreign silk store at No. 782 Jing'an Temple Road was founded by a British woman and hired a Russian named Boros as manager. On the 29th of last month, the manager and the British female store owner went to Yantai together for business. His managerial seat was temporarily replaced by Austrian Ou Sishi Tuolan Na sent by the Huizhong Bank. It happened that at more than 12:00 noon on the 3rd of this month, the store suddenly suffered a fire. At that time, thick smoke filled the air and the fire was blazing. After the firefighters drove to the scene to suck water and extinguish the fire, they also joined the West Patrolmen of the Jing'an Temple Patrol House to conduct a detailed investigation and learned that the store had insured a fire insurance of 52,000 taels of silver and found a lot of flammable materials in the store. It was suspected of arson for insurance money. Therefore, on Saturday last week, the acting manager Austrian Lanna and the store employees Russian Ivan Niko Huoxixuke Inwei Waste Stofski Huoxixuke (same name) and other five people were arrested and taken into the patrol house for detention. This morning, they were escorted to the Criminal Court No. 8 of the First Special District Court. The lawyer of the patrol house, Li Zhishan, stated that the defendants were arrested because they were suspected of arson, but the situation of the case was quite complicated and he requested that the defendants be allowed to be detained and specially interrogated on a later date. When he was asked, the defendant Lanna, an Austrian national aged 41, replied that because the store owner and manager went to Yantai together, he was temporarily replaced by the Huizhong Bank on May 3. The other four defendants (all store employees) left the store for lunch at 12:02 noon and locked the store door. When they returned to the store at about 2 pm, they saw that it was on fire and the firefighters put it out. He did not know how the fire started and he was an Austrian and the patrol house should not arrest him and send him to the Chinese court for trial, etc. He also hired a foreign lawyer to appear in court and apply for bail. In the end, lawyer Li stated that the Austrian consulate had allowed Lanna's detention and Austria had no extraterritoriality, so the court had the right to hear the case and he opposed the bail application because the patrol house was currently investigating the case. Judge Wu Zhuan ordered the case to be specially interrogated on a later date and the defendants were returned to custody.

Ministry of Railways Appoints Huang Zifang as Medical Advisor 186

Also Serves as Head of Health Section for Two Railway Bureaus

The health administration organization of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways originally had a medical director position established outside the Health Section of the General Affairs Department of the Management Bureau. The position of section chief was stipulated to be concurrently held by the medical director. The Health Section only had one administrative section, thus the responsibilities of medical technology and health administration were not clearly distinguished. Recently, the bureau changed its organizational structure, starting with the General Affairs Department, and enhanced the Health Section's organization. This was approved by the Ministry of Railways, changing the administrative section to a clerical section, and adding medical affairs and health care sections. The Ministry of Railways believes that the two railway lines have tens of thousands of employees, and their health is greatly related to work efficiency. Furthermore, the two railway lines have heavy passenger traffic, and the routes pass through many important cities, with the attention of both Chinese and foreigners. Therefore, the public health of all vehicles and stations is of utmost importance. Therefore, a few days ago, the ministry explicitly abolished the position of medical director of the railway lines, and the medical affairs were merged into the Health Section of the General Affairs Department. Dr. Huang Zifang, a medical advisor from the ministry, was appointed as section chief to actively reorganize the section. Huang studied in the United States, received scholarships from the Rockefeller Foundation several times, and served as a Class A medical officer in the Health Section of the League of Nations in Geneva. He has a high reputation in international medicine. Domestically, he has served as the director of the health bureaus of Hankou, Beiping, and other cities, and has rich experience in health administration. After being appointed, Huang has already visited the bureau once and met with Director Huang, Deputy Director Wu, and others. Deng Zhende, the original medical director and head of the Health Section of the General Affairs Department, has been reassigned by the bureau as the director of the Zhenjiang Hospital of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway, to allow him to fully utilize his talents.

Mr. Huang Zifang 187

Appendix: Huang's Curriculum Vitae. Huang Zifang is 35 years old, from Siming, Fujian. He was a second-year medical student at the University of Hong Kong, holds a Bachelor of Science in Physiology and a Master of Science in Public Health and Microbiology from the University of Chicago, and a Doctor of Medicine. He was a public health researcher at Johns Hopkins University, a public health researcher and teaching assistant in microbiology at Harvard University. He received the Rockefeller Foundation Microbiology Scholarship in 1924, and the Rockefeller Foundation Public Health Scholarship in 1928. He is a member of the American Society for Microbiology, the American Society of Parasitologists, the American Association for the Advancement of Science, and the American Public Health Association. He served as a technician, chief of the epidemic prevention section, and chief of the general affairs section at the Central Epidemic Prevention Bureau (1924-1928). He served as the chief of the epidemic prevention section and the health section of the Beiping Health Experimental Zone (1925-1928). He was an honorary professor at Peking Union Medical College (1927-1929) and an honorary professor at Yenching University (1927-1929). He was the director of the Wuhan Special Municipality Health Bureau (1927), and an advisor to the Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau (1928). He was the director of the Beiping Special Municipality Health Bureau (1928-1929). He was a member of the Central Epidemic Prevention Committee (1929), a member of the Central Health Committee (1928-1929), and a member of the Central Labor Health Committee (1929). He was a counselor of the Ministry of Health of the National Government (1929-1930). He was the director of the Hubei Office of the Health Group of the National Government Relief of Flood Disaster Committee (1931-1932). He was a Class A medical officer in the Health Section of the League of Nations in Geneva (1929-1933). He was an executive committee member of the Geneva Branch of the Chinese Nationalist Party (1932-1933).

Workers of the Da Zhong Rubber Factory Petition to Party and Government Agencies 188

The Da Zhong Rubber Factory on Singapore Road, Shanghai West, has over 300 male and female workers. The other day (13th), the factory, in order to oppose the workers' organization of a labor union, implemented a factory closure, preventing workers from entering the factory, causing a major dispute. The workers petitioned the Party, government, and Social Affairs Bureau to send personnel to thoroughly investigate. The details are as follows:

The Truth of the Dispute: According to the factory worker Gu Fengshan, speaking to a reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency, the workers of this factory and the Yi Yuan factory organized the Third District Rubber Union a month ago. The capitalists believed that once the union was established, the workers' interests would be protected and the capitalists would lose the opportunity to mistreat the workers. Therefore, a month and a half ago, Yi Yuan first implemented unjustified layoffs. Now, this factory is doing the same. On the morning of the 13th of this month, the factory closed its doors and posted a notice saying, "All departments temporarily suspend work." Then, it posted a notice dissolving all departments and urging workers to collect their wages. The workers believed that the factory's actions were actually meant to expel them and ignored the notices. The factory then stopped providing food and lodging for the workers. The workers, in this situation, had no choice but to request relief from the authorities.

Petition to the Party and Government: Yesterday morning at 10 a.m., the factory workers specially prepared a document and sent representatives Gu Fengshan, Qiu Haixiong, Chen Jianzhai, Xu Rongjia, Hu Jinbao, Shen Rongquan, Zhou Huihua, and over a hundred others, holding a banner that read "Petition Delegation of Da Zhong Rubber Factory Workers," first went to the Municipal Party Headquarters to petition, requesting that the factory be ordered to resume work immediately. Zhou Lianze, the chief of the civil training section, received them and promised to handle the matter together with the Social Affairs Bureau. Then, they went to the Social Affairs Bureau to petition, requesting immediate mediation to maintain the workers' livelihood. Wang Xianqing, a staff member of the Third Section, received them and promised to immediately send personnel to thoroughly investigate.

Sending Personnel to Thoroughly Investigate: The Social Affairs Bureau, considering that it was already May and to avoid the expansion of the situation, immediately sent Tan Peiyan, a staff member of the Third Section, at 1 p.m. to thoroughly investigate the truth and schedule a meeting between labor and capital representatives at the Social Affairs Bureau for mediation.

Social Affairs Bureau Mediation Yields No Result, Tobacco Workers Union Holds General Meeting Today

Over 7,000 workers from the No. 1 and No. 2 British-American Tobacco factories in Pudong are facing difficulty making a living because the factory has reduced work to only three days a week. Negotiations by the labor union have been unsuccessful. Last Thursday, all child laborers in the leaf tobacco department of the new Pudong factory stopped work. Workers from the No. 3 factory on Taopeng Road also crossed the river to petition. The Fifth District Cigarette Industry Union, fearing the expansion of the unrest, immediately reported the situation to the Party and government agencies, requesting mediation. The Social Affairs Bureau summoned representatives from both labor and capital to the bureau last Friday for negotiations. However, the factory's attitude was firm, and no progress was made. Yesterday (Monday), the new leaf workers had not yet resumed work. The foreign manager of the factory, "Lai Qisheng" (transliteration), directly consulted with the factory's representatives, but the workers were unwilling to work. The union believes that the situation is critical as both sides have taken extreme positions and has scheduled an emergency representative meeting for the 16th to discuss a solution.

Autopsy of Male Corpse Found Dead in Kunshan Garden 190

Around 4 p.m. the day before yesterday, an unidentified male corpse, approximately 20 years old, was discovered in front of House No. 8 behind Kunshan Garden. The Hongkou Police Department was notified and dispatched Chinese and Western detectives to investigate. They found 76 silver dollars and reactionary documents on the corpse. The corpse was taken to the Feilun Road autopsy room, as previously reported. It is now known that the police found the address of the deceased's accomplices in the documents. Detectives went to No. 19 Matterhorn Road and arrested a suspect named Zhu Linqing, who was taken to the police station for temporary detention. Yesterday morning, Zhan Liangce, a prosecutor from the First Special District Court, was commissioned to conduct the autopsy. The autopsy confirmed that the corpse was the deceased, and Zhu Linqing was interrogated. Zhu Linqing confessed that he was from Anhui and did not know the deceased. He also stated that the house on Matterhorn Road was rented by his friend Lao Liu, whose name he did not know. He had only known Liu for a month. Liu had instructed him to live there, saying that a friend would come to him and ask him to take care of him, but he did not reveal the friend's name. Zhan deemed the confession credible and ruled that the unidentified male corpse died from injuries sustained from falling from a high place, resulting in head and leg injuries. As no relatives of the deceased could be found, the body was handed over to the Pushan Shanzhuang for burial.

Mr. Chen Binhe's Speech on National Humiliation Week: September 18th Incident 199

Speech given at the YMCA on May 11th

When talking about the September 18th Incident, we should first talk about Japan's policy towards China. However, Mr. Cai Yuanpei has already spoken about Japan's policy towards China a few days ago, so I won't say much about it here.

Before the Meiji Restoration, Japan was a feudal country. During the Meiji Restoration, it transitioned from a feudal system to a capitalist system, and from an era of isolation to a policy of imperialist expansion. Japan formed its capitalist country under the pressure of advanced imperialism.

In 1853, the American fleet broke through Japan's gates. The Japanese rulers were unwilling to let their country become a colony of the great powers, so they followed the great powers and embarked on the road to capitalism. However, Japan is an island nation, and general industrial construction under capitalism faces the difficulty of lacking raw materials in Japan. Therefore, the Japanese rulers determined two policies of external development in the early years of the Meiji era: one was the southward invasion marine policy, and the other was the northward expansion continental policy. Korea perished under the continental policy, and after that, it was our Northeast's turn. Japan's invasion of the Northeast did not begin with the September 18th Incident, but much earlier, decades ago. After the Sino-Japanese War in the Jiawu year, it broke through the barriers of our Northeast; after the Russo-Japanese War, it strangled the lifeline of our Northeast. For decades, the political and economic aggression of Japanese imperialists in the Northeast has planted deep-rooted forces, causing the mountains and rivers of the Northeast to change color invisibly!

When we talk about the September 18th Incident now, we should know why Japan wanted to launch it. The first motive for launching the September 18th Incident was: Japanese imperialists themselves are an island nation, and in order to develop their capitalist industry, the need for raw materials is very urgent, which has cultivated their ambition to plunder colonies. In recent years, the economic panic of the entire world has of course affected Japan, and various unstable conditions have appeared in society. In order to eliminate the unstable phenomena in the domestic society, and on the other hand, in order to prepare for the second World War, they need a supply of raw materials and a sales market, so they must occupy our Northeast by force! The second is: Japanese imperialism wants to prevent the economic power of the United States from invading our country. The strength of Japanese capital is of course not as strong as that of American capital. It wants to prevent American capital from penetrating our country, which is the mutual conflict between imperialist countries. The third is: Japanese imperialists saw that the Soviet Union's Five-Year Plan was about to succeed, especially the trend of successful industrial socialization in Siberia, which made Japan feel uneasy. The fourth is: China's political instability, coupled with the serious floods in the summer of the year before last. The fifth is the corruption of the Northeast warlords. With these five reasons, Japanese imperialists thought that it was an excellent opportunity to seize the Northeast at this time, so they launched the shocking tragedy on the evening of September 18th of the year before last!

We should also know the situation before the September 18th Incident: In the Wanbaoshan Incident on July 1st of the year before last, Japanese police helped Korean farmers seize the land of Chinese farmers. Chinese farmers refused and rose up to resist, and the Japanese police opened fire and shot Chinese farmers. From July 3rd to 8th, Japan even more planned to instigate Koreans to launch anti-Chinese riots, killing 142 overseas Chinese in Korea, injuring 546, and property losses amounted to more than 4 million Japanese yen. At the same time, they also used the disappearance of Nakamura, a soldier who disguised himself as a spy in the Northeast, as an excuse to launch the Shenyang Incident on September 18th!

After September 18th, Jilin, Heilongjiang, and Jinzhou were also occupied by force; the Tianjin Incident occurred twice on November 8th and 26th; the Shanghai Incident on January 28th of last year; the puppet state of Manchuria was established on March 1st of last year; on December 8th of last year, the Japanese army provoked trouble without reason and shelled Shanhaiguan, and on January 1st of this year, they attacked Yuguan for the second time, and Yuguan was lost again on the afternoon of January 3rd; after February 25th, they attacked Rehe, and Rehe was lost again on March 3rd!

These are some of the biggest things after the September 18th Incident. We still remember them very clearly, so I won't go into detail.

Our current feelings:

The first is that when the September 18th Incident occurred, Zhang Xueliang invented the extremely shameless non-resistance doctrine! Zhang Xueliang could not understand the cause of the September 18th Incident. After the September 18th Incident, he once expressed to others that Japan's invasion of the Northeast was the action of a few Japanese ambitious people and could not represent Japan's entire policy, so his claim was wrong.

We know that Gandhi in India after its fall still made non-violent resistance. Zhang Xueliang is a soldier but advocates non-resistance. If we ask Zhang Xueliang, if other domestic soldiers had sent troops to the Northeast at that time, would he have resisted? I think he would have resisted! Not only would he not want others to seize his territory, but he would not want others to take away his personal belongings at will. But when he left, he had to take away tens of millions of cash and borrow ancient paintings from the Summer Palace in Beiping. This is a painful feeling after the September 18th Incident.

The second feeling is: the so-called "long-term resistance." From non-resistance to long-term resistance, there is not a single achievement made. The so-called "long-term resistance" is really unprepared and has no overall plan! This kind of long-term resistance is equivalent to non-resistance! We know that Jinzhou was lost without resistance; Yuguan was lost without resistance; Rehe was also lost without resistance. The 19th Route Army and 5th Army in the January 28th Incident, as well as Ma Zhanshan and Su Bingwen in the Northeast, and the Northeast Volunteer Army, all resisted without an overall plan and were defeated by the Japanese one by one.

We still remember that after the Sino-Japanese War in the Jiawu year, the local government of Guangdong at that time asked Japan to return the captured warships, saying to the Japanese military authorities: We did not participate in this war, please return the Guangdong warships. This incident was criticized by foreigners, saying that Japan was not at war with China, but with the Qing government; Japan was not at war with the Qing government, but with Li Hongzhang alone! Isn't the resistance of Ma Zhanshan, Su Bingwen, the 19th Route Army, and the Northeast Volunteer Army just Japan fighting with Ma Zhanshan personally! With Su Bingwen personally! Japan is only fighting with a part of the 19th Route Army! (To be continued)

Unveiling Ceremony of Deng Keng's Bronze Statue Made by Li Jinfat 201

Last year, Chen Jitang, Commander-in-Chief of the First Army Group, initiated the construction of a bronze statue of Deng Keng to commemorate him. At that time, Chairman Chiang also donated 10,000 yuan to help its completion. The statue was contracted to sculptor Li Jinfat, and the work took a year to complete. May 5th was specially chosen as the date for the unveiling ceremony. The ceremony was very grand. In addition to Chen Jitang, who was absent due to the Yantang military parade, those who attended the ceremony included Liu Jiwen, He Luo, Lin Shiqing, Li Xian'gen, Zhang Zhiying, Luo Yiqun, Chen Fuchu, Lu Yougang, Huo Guanghe, and Deng Keng's family, as well as over 300 guests. The ceremony began with the Director of Public Security, He Luo, unveiling the Party and National flags of the bronze statue. The Commander of the Military Police, Lin Shiqing, reported Deng Keng's life story. Representatives from the Political Affairs Committee, Luo Yiqun, Li Jinfat, Deng Shizhang, and others gave speeches. Then, congratulatory messages from all walks of life were read. The statue is ten feet tall, made of bronze color, and its expression is vivid and closely resembles the person. It stands on a fifteen-foot-tall stone base with new-style carvings, erected in the square in front of the Guangzhou-Kowloon Railway Station. It is the first domestic bronze statue in Guangzhou.

Then Director Gu delivered a speech, stating that the Ministry of Education has paid great attention to Muslim education in recent years and that the establishment of the committee is closely related to education and educational administration. He hoped that the members of the committee would provide assistance at any time. After that, they began to discuss and pass the organizational outline, budget, and declaration, and mutually elected Chu Minyi, Tang Kesan, and Sun Shengwu as standing committee members.

Middle School Teachers' Association Initiates the Organization of a National Middle School Teachers' Association 206

Gathering Strength to Assist the Government in Saving the Nation from Peril

Connecting the Middle School Education Community to Jointly Seek Appropriate Progress

The Shanghai Municipal Middle School Teachers' Union yesterday issued a letter soliciting opinions from middle schools across the country on the organization of a National Middle School Teachers' Union. The original text is as follows: To the faculty and staff of middle schools across the country: Today's China is on the verge of destruction. Internally, the communist bandits are rampant in the southern countryside, collapsing without any remainder; externally, the Japanese invaders are swallowing up our Northeast, and the powerful nations are all coveting our market. The country is shattered like this, something never seen before in our history. The tidal wave of global economic panic will lead to the outbreak of a second World War. In this boiling cauldron, the nation's survival hangs by a thread, and yet many of our compatriots are still sound asleep. Although patriotic people are everywhere, they suffer from a lack of unity and are ultimately unable to shoulder the heavy responsibility of saving the country. They can only watch as the government struggles, internal worries become increasingly serious, and external troubles intensify. The Association is aware of this and believes that if our compatriots across the country rise up quickly to jointly avert the crisis, how can the country's future be considered? In particular, our colleagues in the education sector are outstanding members of the country. After ten years of recuperation and ten years of education, the responsibility of saving the country must be at the forefront. For more than ten years, the student community has been enthusiastic about the patriotic movement and has achieved some success, but our middle school teachers and staff have not made any statement. Shouldn't we feel ashamed? There are no less than a thousand middle schools across the country, and the number of middle school teachers and staff is even uncountable. However, we have never heard of any organization, let alone anything else. The rise and fall of the country is the responsibility of every citizen, let alone us outstanding intellectuals? Moreover, at this time of deep water and scorching fire, saving the country through education is a fundamental plan. In particular, secondary education connects the past and the future, and its mission is especially important. Seeing this, the unity of our middle school teachers and staff is an urgent task at present. In order to meet the urgent needs of the environment, the Association has initiated the organization of a National Middle School Teachers' Union in order to: 1. Gather strength to assist the government in saving the country from peril and strive to survive; 2. Connect middle schools across the country, which have no organization, to jointly seek the advancement of education. Colleagues of middle schools in various places who sympathize with this proposal are earnestly requested to come to the Association to jointly plan for unity and strive for survival.

Siam Education Delegation Visits Jinan University 207

President Zheng Hongnian Hosts a Banquet

Hoping Siam Treats Overseas Chinese Equally

According to the Kwok Man News Agency, the Siam Education Delegation, which came to China to investigate the state of education, arrived in Shanghai a few days ago. Yesterday (the 15th) at 8:00 AM, members of the delegation, such as Phya Wisutra, Secretary-General of the Siam Ministry of Education, Chen Wentian, President of the Siam Chinese-Language Kuo Min Jih Pao, and overseas Chinese businessmen Chen Yian, Lin Weilie, and Liu Lengqiao, and seven others visited Jinan University in Zhenru. Zheng Hongnian, the president of the university, and all the faculty and students warmly welcomed them. After the memorial service, they introduced Phya Wisutra, Chen Wentian, and Liu Lengqiao to speak about the significance of their visit to the country and the situation of overseas Chinese in Siam. Later, Yang Yufen, the secretary-general of the university, accompanied them on a tour of various parts of the university. The Siam Overseas Chinese Student Association and the Nanyang Cultural Enterprise Department of the university also held a tea party at No. 5 Yuntao Hall. President Zheng hosted a banquet at 12:00 noon on the third floor of the Guanshengyuan Restaurant on Nanjing Road, and invited reporters from various newspapers to attend. During the banquet, President Zheng delivered a speech briefly describing the close relationship between China and Siam in history, almost like brothers. He said that in the past ten years, Siam's politics have been on track and the country has made great progress in everything. China expresses its deep sympathy. The current Siamese government's increase in overseas Chinese donations and compulsory education regulations are actually detrimental to overseas Chinese in various ways. He hoped that the Siamese government would treat our overseas Chinese compatriots equally, and that our overseas Chinese compatriots would also be able to help the Siamese government to promote the progress of Siam. The friendship between the Chinese and Siamese peoples should be based on the communication of education and culture, and we should work hard from this point. Phya Wisutra replied in English, saying that he would report his good impressions of his visit to China to his government and request that it reduce the time for teaching Siamese in Chinese schools as much as possible, so that Chinese students can learn more Chinese.

Henan University Education Delegation 211

Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday | Plans to Stay for Two Days

The Henan University Education Delegation set off from Kaifeng at the beginning of last month, passing through Dingxian, Beiping, Tianjin, Jinan, Zouping, Nanjing, Zhenjiang, Wuxi, Suzhou, and other places, and arrived in Shanghai last night. They are staying at Shanghai Middle School. There are a total of twelve male and female members, led by their professor, Dr. Tai Shuangqiu. The delegation has three goals: to visit school education, to investigate rural education, and to promote the local products movement. There are five aspects to their work: advocating local products to save the country, visiting famous schools, investigating practical education, investigating rural construction, and collecting rural economic research data. It is planned that after returning to Bian, they will conduct an experiment on an "education village" near Kaifeng, based on an economic perspective, and integrate education into economic construction. It is also reported that when Mr. Tai lectured on the local products movement in various places, the audience was very moved and many shed tears. In Wuxi, he also proposed that various places automatically organize "Nian Er Societies," with the aim of promoting local products, practicing social frugality, striving for social production, and working together to save the Chinese nation from danger and solve the people's livelihood from the 22nd year of the Republic of China. Comrades in various places are communicating and soliciting opinions. The general communication office is located at Henan University in Kaifeng.

Hongkou Open-Air Swimming Pool Opened Yesterday 215

No Less Than Five Hundred Water Enthusiasts

The Hongkou open-air swimming pool, established by the Shanghai Municipal Council, opened at 6:00 AM yesterday. The reporter arrived in time and saw a sea of heads (exposed on the water surface), no less than five hundred. Water enthusiasts such as Yin Yanjun, Yu Binqi, Wang Jianxin, and Bao Lengxue were as vigorous as in previous years, circling endlessly in the pool. Unexpectedly, the weather did not cooperate, with thunder and lightning and heavy rain. If it were any other sport, it would have ruined the fun, but in this case, there was no worry at all. They even regarded it as a fountain bestowed by heaven and instead increased the fun a lot. Ordinary water enthusiasts were even more active. The most ridiculous thing at this time was a drowned chicken that jumped in from the door. Although it had not yet swam, it was no different from those in the water, as these people had already received the grace of God halfway through. Today is Tuesday (according to the regulations, tickets are 50 cents each, and three tickets are one dollar, but on Tuesdays and Fridays, they are sold at a reduced price of 20 cents). It is expected that the number of people going to quench their swimming thirst will be several times more than yesterday.

Third Shanghai International Games Set for June 3rd and 4th 230

Women's Team as Official Championship Adding 1000m Steeplechase and Women's Javelin, Deadline for Registration in All Countries is May 29th

The third Shanghai International Games have been decided to be held on June 3rd and 4th at the China Athletic Field. Yesterday, the Association convened a meeting of representatives from various countries at the YMCA. More than ten representatives from various countries were present, and Chairman Shen Siliang recorded the resolutions as follows:

Conference Dates and Registration Period 231

The conference dates were set for June 3rd and 4th. If it rains, it will be postponed for one week to June 10th and 11th. The registration deadline is May 29th, Monday, at 6:00 PM at the China Sports Association. When the date was decided, the German and Russian representatives said that it conflicted with the rowing association date, but because changing it later might be too hot, they expressed sympathy but could not agree.

Women's Team as Official Championship 232

In the past two years, the women's team was only an exhibition game. Starting this year, it will be an official championship competition with the same events, but adding the javelin event. There was an initial proposal to add the discus event, but the javelin was considered more suitable, so it was adopted. The events are 50m, 100m, 200m, relay, high jump, long jump, and javelin.

Add 1000m Steeplechase and Women's Javelin 233

The women's team will add the javelin event. In the men's team, there was an initial proposal to add the 1000m steeplechase, but it was finally decided to temporarily make it an exhibition game. Mike McKenna was recommended to plan everything because Mike has a lot of experience in this area. The exhibition date is June 3rd. Although the steeplechase is one of the world's Olympic events, it is rare for Chinese people to practice it.

Cancel Individual Participation 234

Cancel individual participation. All must participate on behalf of their country. Even one athlete can represent the country.

Prizes Not to Exceed 20 Yuan 235

The prizes for the Games are too extravagant and lose their true meaning. In order to promote true technical competition, it was decided that the silver cup for the first place should not exceed 20 yuan (the previous year was 50 yuan). The prizes for the second, third, and fourth places are medals.

Recommend Wang Zhengting as the chairman of the conference. The members of the other committees are recommended as follows:

Free Talk

Children Demand Novelty 243

— Xuan

The newspaper on the 10th of this month carried an advertisement from the Children's Bookstore, stating that someone was "infringing on legal interests" under the name of "New Children's Bookstore." The legal interpretation of this matter is not the focus of this article. What we should pay attention to is that the promotion of children's books in the book industry is also very competitive.

The result of business competition should be improved products. However, we often only see imitation and crude manufacturing. Thirty years ago, Chinese children's books only included a few volumes such as "The Catless Country." Now, in addition to bookstores specializing in publishing children's books, large and small bookstores are printing a large number of children's books. In terms of "quantity," it is undeniable that there is progress, but can the "quality" be satisfactory? In the past, when there were only fairy tales such as "Thumbelina" and "The Catless Country," there were no "comic strip novels," so those few fairy tales were "exclusive." Now, the number of children's books is thousands of times greater, but it cannot prevent the ubiquitous "comic strip novels." On this point, the new book industry and the authors of children's books should reflect deeply!

There are now perhaps 10,000 different kinds of children's books of varying levels, but "comic strip novels" number at most only a few hundred. However, the latter's circulation and appeal far exceed the former. This phenomenon is alarming. Most of today's children's books are literary. They can be roughly divided into three categories: one is simple stories about cat brothers and dog brothers, either translated, written, or adapted from Chinese folk tales; the target audience is children aged seven or eight. The second is more complex, but the themes are mostly still in the first category, with occasional historical legends and myths. The third is translations of Western literary classics, such as Treasure Island. According to this classification, we know that the first and second categories have differences in complexity but no essential difference. The third category suddenly jumps higher, especially in terms of language. If the first and second categories are suitable for children aged eight to ten, then the third category is suitable for first or second year junior high school students aged fourteen or fifteen. Therefore, children aged twelve or thirteen simply have no books to read. I believe this is one of the reasons why "comic strip novels" are so popular among fifth and sixth grade elementary school students.

Secondly, although there are many of the first and second categories of books mentioned above, the content is very thin. Whether it is a Western story or a domestic story, it is the same old stuff that everyone uses, resulting in identical content. Therefore, even seven or eight-year-old children feel a lack of reading material. "Just a few stories copied over and over!" Seven or eight-year-old children are dissatisfied with new books. So he also learns from his older brother and starts reading "comic strip novels."

Therefore, as far as elementary children's books are concerned, the current problem is not a shortage of books, but rather that the content of the books is repeatedly copied and lacks fresh themes. This is exactly the opposite of the problem with advanced children's books!

Returning to the Children's Bookstore. The Children's Bookstore does not publish many books, but in my opinion, it has one characteristic: the 101-volume Children's Science Series. In today's market flooded with literary children's books, the mere 101-volume Children's Science Series can be considered a drop in the bucket. If someone follows suit and competes in this area, it might not be a bad thing, as long as they are willing to seriously hire people to write and not crudely manufacture, imitate, and profit.

Digging Underground Shelters 244

— Da Wu

When Japanese planes arrived in Peiping, our army still said, "Resist to the end." Naturally, the people had no choice but to flee quickly. Tickets for the Pingpu Railway increased by more than double the usual amount in one day, and even more the next day. The station was extremely crowded. This was truly a booming business!

But some people did not flee and instead dug underground shelters. The elementary schools in Peiping, in order to ensure the safety of their students, sent representatives to the Social Affairs Bureau to petition and suspended classes for half a day to dig underground shelters (Shen Bao, Peiping Special Dispatch, 11th). The content of the petition probably wanted to ask the authorities to include the elementary school students in the fifth batch of antiques being packed and transported, and to take the train south. It is pitiful that the antiques have already been transported in five batches, but the elementary school students have only just dug underground shelters, preparing to burrow underground to escape. Compared to the fact that some people copied wills, copper boxes, stone boxes, built pagodas, and treasured things before the Japanese planes followed the antiques south, what are our feelings?

But I remembered the Japanese army's retreat from Luandong a few days earlier. Some people speculated that the reason for the retreat was one of three: first, the Japanese army's forces were not strong, and our army's defense was solid; second, the war was approaching foreign interests in Luandong; and third, the strategy was changed to threaten Tianjin and Peiping. But I myself speculate that the dwarfs were imitating Dong Shi, trying to "lure the enemy in deep."

But at that time, it was said that the refugees in Luandong were returning one after another, "and gradually resuming business" (Shen Bao Special Dispatch, April 29), and the newspapers also carried "breaking," "expelling," "advancing," "recapturing," and "occupying" and other joyful words in large and small characters. It was as if the Chinese people had gone from a miserable life to a good life, although under the protection of foreigners, it was also the result of our army's resistance against Japan.

However, the great cause of resisting Japan is difficult to predict. The newspapers clearly carried "recapturing" and "occupying," but suddenly it "clearly did not match the facts." It turned out that our army only had "very few troops going to 囗囗 and other county towns to maintain local order and safe traffic" and did not "attack the Japanese army." Therefore, as soon as the enemy provoked, Dolon fell, Japanese planes arrived in Peiping, and elementary school students dug underground shelters, like rabbits, escaping underground.

Now is the time to save the country through aviation. With airplanes, it is naturally quick to escape. But it is inconvenient to drag many elementary school students along, so we have to dig underground shelters, bury them underground, for safekeeping. Although the Japanese bombs are fierce, what can they do when the Chinese people escape into the sky and dive into the earth, and even the antiques have already been transported clean, leaving only a few young children in the underground shelter?

Coal 245

— Zhou Lengjia

The Huangpu River, the turbid river water flows continuously all day long. The Goddess of Peace statue on the riverside frowned and looked down. The artillery positions of an aircraft carrier were aimed at her.

Machines are roaring, motors are vibrating, and the small coal worker is carrying a basket of coal weighing one hundred and twenty pounds on his shoulder.

The sky is overcast, the air is full of moisture, and the air pressure is low, making it difficult to breathe.

"Hang yu! Hang yu!" A burst of depressed cries squeezed out, broke through the gloomy air on the riverside, and several tanned, muscular arms were raised upwards. A heavy basket of coal was pressed onto Afu's shoulders again.

Afu, a young man who was squeezed out of the countryside, has been working as a coal carrier on the riverside for two months.

For two months, he has been carrying coal from trucks all day long, carrying it in a running posture, to the tall riverboats. The coal baskets are heavy, pressing his back down and making his ribs ache faintly, but he still has to carry it, still has to move it.

The woman on the billboard, smoking, is leisurely looking at him with a smile, laughing at him for being stupid. Yes, he is stupid, but if he is not stupid, he will not have anything to eat. Poor humans are destined to squeeze out their sweat and blood to exchange for food.

Sweat is flowing, blood is flowing, and his ribs are aching. No one pities him, only those baskets of coal, as if they are against him, are constantly transported by trucks to the riverside to weigh down his shoulders.

It seems that there is an endless amount of coal produced in this world, and he will never be able to transport it all in his lifetime.

"Hey, what a mess! Four cents a day, I have to carry more than a hundred baskets of coal. One day, I'll be crushed to death!" Sometimes he really can't stand it anymore, and he will grumble a few words, but when he thinks of life, when he thinks of the pain of being hungry, he finally just swallows a mouthful of saliva and quietly gathers his strength, squats down, and waits for his companions to lift a basket of coal and press it onto his shoulders. He is content, he does not hope to have any delicacies in his mouth, he just needs a few big pancakes, fried bread sticks, and glutinous rice balls a day.

His dreams are comfortable, he does not hope to have any woman in his arms, he just needs a place to sleep, whether it is a slum or an open-air cement floor, he will fall asleep peacefully.

But, unfair things finally came to him.

One day, just as he was carrying coal onto a riverboat in a running posture, his foot suddenly stepped on a banana peel on the riverbank and slipped. As a result, a basket of coal weighing one hundred and twenty pounds fell down and pressed on his back, covering him with coal dust. The force of this pressure was really not light, making the inside of his body feel as if he had been stabbed with a knife, and he involuntarily spat out a mouthful of blood.

He raised his head and looked towards the boat. On the deck of the riverboat, there was a young couple leaning against the railing, talking passionately, while peeling bananas and putting them into their mouths, as if they didn't know that a tragic scene they had created was happening under the boat.

He couldn't help but take a breath of cold air, and a surge of anger surged:

"Damn it! I'm really going to die, just to make you two happy!"

But he didn't dare to run up and hit them, to take revenge. He just endured the pain and climbed back to the slum where he lived.

That night, he was in so much pain that he clutched his chest and cried out, shedding tears all night.

The next day, when his companions continued to go to the riverside to do the coal carrying work as usual, Afu was nowhere to be seen. No one knew where he had gone.

One day, two days, the days flew by like arrows, and Afu was never seen again. Only everything on the riverside remained the same: the Goddess of Peace was frowning and looking down, the woman on the billboard was smoking and smiling, the sirens on the riverboats were roaring, the roof of the Sassoon Building was shining with golden light, and other small coal workers were still working in the cloudy sky and gloomy air.

Ramblings from the Qu Cottage 246

— Zizhan

(28) Pacify the Interior? Resist the Exterior?

The late Qing authorities were ignorant and incompetent. In foreign affairs, they did not hesitate to cede power and humiliate the country, while in domestic affairs, they feared the expansion of civil rights. On the one hand, they strongly rejected the earnest requests of the constitutionalists, and on the other hand, they brutally suppressed the revolutionaries. The members of that group harbored the selfish desire to "rather give to friends than to family slaves," believing that pacifying the interior was more important than resisting the exterior. In the end, because the exterior could not be resisted, the interior became even more difficult to pacify, and the Qing Dynasty collapsed. I believe that the demise of the Ming and Qing Dynasties was the same. The national policy of the late Ming Dynasty was defeated by corrupt officials. Factional strife arose frequently, seeking to satisfy personal desires: strong enemies were not resisted, and making deals was the plan. When the Manchurian soldiers swept through North China and approached Jiangnan, the small Nanjing court still had disputes over pacifying the interior or resisting the exterior, and they could not agree. The treacherous officials Ma Shiying, Ruan Dacheng, and others strongly advocated prioritizing pacifying the interior and suppressing the rebellious forces of Zuo Liangyu. The military strength in Jiangnan was insufficient, so they even withdrew troops from Jiangbei to defend against foreign aggression to reinforce it. At that time, the Manchurian soldiers were advancing south day by day. Yao Sixiao, the Vice Minister of the Court of Judicial Review, and the censors Qiao Kepin and Cheng Youqian requested that the Jiangbei troops not be withdrawn and that Yangzhou be defended urgently. Shiying scolded loudly: "You Donglin, you are still using Jiang Defense as an excuse, wanting to let the rebellious Zuo invade? If the northern soldiers arrive, we can still negotiate a deal: if the rebellious Zuo arrives, then you high officials and our emperor will die alone." Sixiao and others, fearing severe punishment, dared not discuss resisting foreign aggression. The defenses of Huaiyang became weaker, and the Manchurian soldiers marched straight in, massacred Yangzhou, captured Nanjing, and captured King Fu. It can be said that the Ming Dynasty died because it specialized in internal warfare and did not resist foreign enemies. Pacify the interior? Resist the exterior? The authorities are confused, but the bystanders are clear. We were born after the Ming and Qing Dynasties, and when we discuss why the Ming and Qing Dynasties perished, why should we worry about having no words to write?

Carrot Hair 247

— Jules Kenaru, translated by Lin Quzuo

Agathe (continued)

Lepique had almost finished his bread. This time, Agathe didn't let him get ahead. She focused all her attention on Lepique, forgetting everyone else, until Mrs. Lepique coldly said:

"Agathe, what are you doing?"

That's what reminded her.

"I'm here, Madam," Agathe answered.

She watched Lepique even more intently. She wanted to conquer him with her solicitude, and try to get his attention.

She didn't miss the opportunity.

When Lepique was chewing the last bite of bread, she rushed to the sideboard, took a ring loaf weighing five kilograms that hadn't been cut, and offered it to him very sincerely, feeling very pleased with herself for guessing the master's need.

But Lepique took off his napkin, left the table, put on his hat, and went to the garden to smoke.

When he had finished eating, he wouldn't eat any more.

Agathe stood there holding the five-kilogram ring loaf, as still as a wax figure advertising a life raft factory.

Rules

"This upsets you," Carrot Hair said to Agathe when only the two of them were left in the kitchen. "But don't be discouraged, there are even more upsetting things to come. Where are you taking those wine bottles?"

"To the cellar, Mr. Carrot Hair."

Carrot Hair said:

"I'm sorry, only I'm allowed to go into the cellar. The stairs are completely broken, women can't keep their footing, they'll break their necks, but I've earned everyone's trust since the day I could walk down the stairs. I can tell the difference between the red and blue labels on the wine bottles in there.

"I sell the small wine barrels we've used, getting a little extra money, and I sell the rabbit skins too. I give the money I make to Mum.

"Let's get this straight now, to avoid hindering each other later when we're working.

"In the morning, I let the dog out and give him breakfast. In the evening, I whistle to call him in to sleep. When he wanders around and comes back late, I have to wait for him.

"Also, Mum has told me to close the henhouse door every day.

"I go outside to find weeds that aren't poisonous, pull them up by the roots, knock the dirt off on my feet, fill in the holes I pulled them out of, and then bring the weeds back to feed the rabbits.

"I help Dad saw wood, as exercise.

"I'm the one who kills the game that Dad brings back but hasn't killed, and then you and sister Elestine pluck the feathers.

"I'm also responsible for cleaning the fish, I dig out everything from the fish's belly, and stomp on the swim bladder with my foot.

"But scraping off the scales and fetching water from the well is your job.

"I help people untangle tangled skeins of thread.

"I grind coffee." (Unsold)

The gold market yesterday saw the swap trading market heated with short covering. Silk and Tea: Good Spring Silkworm Development in Jiangsu and Zhejiang 262

(Wuxian) Suzhou's Hushu Pass, Hengjing, Mubin, Xukou, and other areas are famous silkworm breeding areas with numerous seed production farms. In recent years, although silkworm farming in neighboring counties has failed due to unfavorable weather conditions, Suzhou's silk production has not been too bad, thanks to the assistance and guidance of students from the Hushu Pass Girls' Sericulture School and the Suzhou Agricultural School. This year, many farmers are raising improved breeds. The number of silkworms being raised in Renqiao and Xincun areas, which have cooperated with the Suzhou Agricultural School, has increased compared to last year. The weather is sunny and warm, and development is smooth. The early batch of silkworms has been fed leaves for many days, and the late batch is still beginning to sleep. There is no market for mulberry leaves.

(Shangyu) In recent years, farmers have been discouraged by the failure of silkworm farming. This year, there is a panic in the rural economy, and there is no need to buy seeds. They have all borrowed funds from the township public offices to purchase improved breeds for breeding. However, the silkworms are not developing well. The number of silkworms being raised in townships such as Zhangzhen and Shangpu is relatively large. The early batch has been fed for three sleeps, and then released to eat leaves. The late silkworms are still in the second sleep. The mulberry trees in the four townships are producing abundant leaves, and the supply exceeds demand. The price of leaves is surprisingly cheap, only 0.3-0.4 yuan per load. In another week, all the silkworms will be ready to spin cocoons.

Spring and Autumn

Wu Proverbs: Casual Notes 270

— Shanlu

In Wu proverbs, derogatory terms for people have varying degrees of severity! For example, to criticize someone for being dirty, simply saying "dirty" is a mild derogatory term; going a step further is "dirty inside dirty," which becomes a severe derogatory term. To laugh at someone for being muddled, simply saying "muddled" is a mild derogatory term; going a step further is "muddled inside muddled," which becomes a severe derogatory term. By analogy, simply saying "amateur," "awkward," "clumsy," "long-winded," 「Note」 are all mild derogatory terms; if the intensity is increased, they become "amateur inside amateur," "awkward inside awkward," "clumsy inside clumsy," "long-winded inside long-winded," all becoming severe derogatory terms. From this, I have derived a formula: whenever an adjective is repeated with the addition of the character "inside," it indicates unsatisfactory criticism and is not applicable to satisfactory criticism. There is only "dirty inside dirty," not "clean inside clean"; only "muddled inside muddled," not "clear inside clear"; only "amateur inside amateur," not "professional inside professional"; only "clumsy inside clumsy," not "neat inside neat"; only "long-winded inside long-winded," not "concise inside concise." It is evident that even common sayings and idioms have certain textual rules.

Satisfactory criticism transforms a two-character adjective into a four-character adjective, using only a reduplication method. For example, "dry and clean," "clear and refreshing," "neat and tidy," "simple and concise" are all adjectives transformed from two to four characters. This usage is also applicable to unsatisfactory criticism; one can say "dirty inside dirty," and also "dirty dirty"; one can say "muddled inside muddled," and also "muddled muddled"; other cases can be deduced by analogy. 「Dirty dirty," "muddled muddled" are only mild derogatory terms; slightly different from the severe derogatory terms "muddled inside muddled" and "dirty inside dirty."

"Note" The common term for lengthy speech is "long-winded"; in fact, it is merely a mispronunciation of "intertwined," "long-winded inside long-winded" is equivalent to "intertwined inside intertwined"; "long-winded long-winded" is equivalent to "intertwined intertwined."

So Modern 271

— Yimei

The comedian Xu Zhuodai, signing his name to humorous and delightful works, resided in Hongxingfang, Zhabei, and thus called himself "Xu Gong of Zhabei," cleverly replacing the "city" character of "Xu Gong of the North City." Later, Zhuodai moved to Jiangwan, and Xu Bibo lived near Hengbang Bridge, so he ceded the title of "Master of Zhabei" to Bibo, also signing "Old Xu the Half-Old" and "Master of the Broken Night Kettle Room," all of which were enough to elicit laughter. Recently, he has even called himself "Modern Old Man," which is also quite wonderful.

In Suzhou, there is a village called Hengjing. The local people's pronunciation of "dong" is like "deng," "feng" is like "fen," and "tong" is like "teng." The maid hired by my family is from Hengjing. Coincidentally, the maid living opposite is also from Hengjing. Knowing each other in a foreign land, they are unusually close. This morning, I was still in bed, reluctant to get up, when I heard my family's maid talking to the maid living opposite in front of the door. I was upstairs, separated by a window, so I couldn't hear clearly what they were talking about. I only heard my family's maid opening her mouth to say "modern," and closing her mouth to say "modern." The maid living opposite also used "modern" in her sentences. I couldn't help but be greatly surprised, thinking that the word "modern" is the catchphrase of fashionable people. Could it be that these women from remote villages also understand the accents of fashionable people? Upon closer listening, I realized that it was not the case. It turned out that today the one who empties the chamber pots was on strike and did not come, causing the excrement to overflow and be difficult to dispose of. The maid was anxious about this and worked hard to solve the chamber pot problem. "Modern" is the Hengjing people's pronunciation of "chamber pot."

Poor Talk 272

— Yongzi

"Not afraid of ferocity, only afraid of poverty." Poor people are worth less than Pekingese dogs in the world. Unexpectedly, someone is afraid of them. It is truly an honor that one never dreamed of.

That's right. The "Imperial Army," which was fiercely invincible during the Battle of Shanghai, was defeated by a few hand grenades. Only those who have been poor their whole lives, once they become traitors, are like June stink bugs and mosquitoes, making people shudder at the sight.

There are many examples in the world of people being afraid of the poor. One cold day, a friend and I were walking along a certain road when suddenly a poor man wearing torn clothes followed my friend, addressing him as "old pal." Although my friend denied it vehemently, he eventually dug into his pocket. From then on, he dared not walk that road again, saying he was afraid of running into that poor kid again.

Indeed, poor people, having no other way to go, are capable of anything. If soft tactics don't work, hard tactics will. First comes a blackmail letter, then kidnapping and ransom, not afraid of the big shots with puffed-up chests and protruding bellies.

The proletariat has already been tainted with seven parts poverty. If the proletariat loses their jobs again, they will be completely poor without any discounts, making them fearful to others, thus standing tall and firm. Therefore, civilized countries around the world have to rack their brains to find ways to solve the problem of "unemployment relief." Even your esteemed Republic of China is loudly promoting plans for "rural revitalization" because farmers are extremely poor.

"Unemployment relief" and "rural revitalization" are for what? To be blunt, isn't it because they are afraid of the "poor" rebelling?

However, to be poor enough to make people afraid, one must at least be poor to the point of recklessness and disregard for life. Like me, even though I am shameless enough to talk "poor talk," I am still unwilling to risk my life. If one is unwilling to risk one's life, no one will be afraid. Among the readers, there must be like-minded people who, like me, want both money and life, so they should never dream of being touched by "poverty" and making others afraid.

Long Novel

Fourth Company Commander of the Northeast 273

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Six: Sweet and Bitter Love Scene, Coldly Observing Both Sides, Treacherous Worldly Path, Secret Agreement for Three Years

Guizhi lowered her head, playing with the copper spoon, and said, "I feel I'm much more open-minded now. If it were two years ago, you could have killed me, and I still wouldn't have come to a coffee shop." Jizhi said, "Thank you, thank you, I'm glad you're willing to do me the honor, but I hope you'll do me the honor to the end." Guizhi said, "What do you mean by doing you the honor to the end?" Jizhi leaned his arms on the table, looked at her with a sincere expression, and said seriously, "It's easy to understand, it's about what I'm asking for…" Then he smiled and said, "That's not how to put it, it's about what I said earlier, the three-year agreement. What do you think about that? Please give me a definite answer. If you can wait, that would be wonderful. But if you say the worldly path is treacherous…" Guizhi raised her chin and said, "There! You're saying that again. If you're sincere, what does it matter if the world is treacherous? I'll just follow this path, cross the barriers when they come, and cross the bridges when they're there, and see where it leads. You haven't even started, and you're already afraid you can't get through? That won't do! Alright! I know what you mean." As she spoke, she stood up, pushed the bowl and copper spoon in front of her forward, and stood up, holding the table. Her face was tight, facing the door, as if she were about to leave. Jizhi quickly stood up, went to the door, and blocked her, saying, "Please don't be impatient, let's talk it over slowly." Guizhi said, "I've been out for so long, I'm afraid my mom will call me, I have to go back and check." Jizhi stretched out his hands and blocked the door, saying, "But we haven't made a decision yet. Can you sit down for five more minutes? Or have another cup of tea like that day?" Guizhi frowned and said, "I really have to go back, I can't delay. Didn't you say we'll talk it over slowly? That's easy, we'll talk it over slowly." Seeing that she was always facing outward, without turning around, and that blocking her way like this might make her think he was forcing her, Jizhi said, "If you have something to do, I won't insist, but we haven't finished talking today. Maybe tomorrow, maybe the day after, we can come here and talk again, what do you think?" Guizhi nodded and said, "Okay." (71)

Fashion of the Times 274

— Ke Ding'an

Today, when the nation is in crisis, we, the general public, are trying our best to find ways to save the country, like "saving the country through aviation," "saving the country through military affairs," and even "saving the country through dance" and "saving the country through entertainment." I believe that the most important and crucial thing is "saving the country through domestic goods," which everyone can practice without any preparation or training. The public only needs to hold the firm belief that "I will only buy domestic goods from now on." Slowly, from near to far, one person does it, a hundred people follow, and the entire nation practices it in the same way. Then domestic goods will become widespread throughout the country, producers will produce endlessly, and consumers will buy endlessly. At that time, our economy will be strong, and all foreign aggressions will naturally disappear.

The China National Products Company, which aims to save the country through domestic goods, has seen that people in modern centers always seek foreign goods for clothing. If this is not used as a lesson, the sales of foreign goods will only increase in the future. Therefore, they resolutely held a fashion show that shocked all of Shanghai. They invited many movie stars, such as Hu Die, Xu Lai, Gao Qingping, Ai Xia, Xuan Jinglin, and Hu Ping, Gu Haijun, and other ladies to perform the fashion show. During the three-day session, no less than 30,000 of Shanghai's noble ladies participated. It was truly "fragrant clothing and beautiful hairpins, and a myriad of wonders."

In the fashion shows performed by the stars, their clothing materials were made of silk, wool, and cloth. The types of fashion included coats, long gowns, short coats, vests, Western suits, and various original clothing. The most striking was the short black satin top and semi-long pants worn by Hu Die, trimmed with white and red interwoven lace. The collar was a pull-over style, and the pant legs were also trimmed with the same lace. The waist was tied with a red, white, and black interwoven silk belt, which had an oriental flavor. When she came out, the applause was like thunder.

Xu Lai wore a dress made of red and white willow pattern georgette on top and red and yellow large floral georgette on the bottom. The shoulders were covered with lotus leaf-style capes, and the waist was pleated. Walking around, she could stretch her feet very well. It was also suitable for everyday wear. Ms. Ai Xia's long coat and short vest, and Gu Meijun's fine-waisted, chest-knotted, bare-shouldered dress also revealed a natural beauty. Xuan Jinglin's white satin long dress and Hu Ping's light green Indian silk bare-shoulder short-sleeved clothing all expressed their personality.

It is said that this fashion show "used silk, wool, and cloth to make more than 90 sets, costing more than 3,000 yuan." I know that such great publicity will surely win the sympathy of noble ladies and will no longer buy foreign goods.

Wandering in the Arts

Dramatized Educational Films 275

Film is the eighth art. The reason why it is listed after painting, music, dance, drama, sculpture, novels, and poetry is that its history is shorter than other arts, but its impact on society is greater than any other art. Therefore, all Western countries are doing their best to operate the film industry. Italy and the Soviet Union are using films to promote various new constructions.

The decline of Chinese culture and the prevalence of illiteracy are undeniable facts. Eliminating illiteracy is a major obstacle to building a new China, but eliminating illiteracy cannot be done in a short period of time. To achieve quick results, one can only start with film. I believe that film is a powerful tool for transforming society and an instrument for promoting culture.

In the past, filmmakers regarded film as a form of entertainment for people to pass the time, so they only sought to cater to the low-level psychology of the general audience. In fact, film is not just for entertainment; it must contain educational and cultural significance. Recently, filmmakers have realized the great mission that film bears to society and have abandoned the "martial arts" and "supernatural" films that are guaranteed to make money, and have come to produce anti-feudal and revolutionary films. Undoubtedly, they have made a significant change in the selection of film scripts.

In the work plan of the China Educational Film Association, there is a concrete provision for the mission that film should bear. Its outline is: (A) Promote the national spirit. (1) Show the advantages of Eastern culture; promote the glory of Chinese history; (3) Show the process of the national revolution. (B) Encourage production and construction. (1) Shift from urban to rural areas; (2) Promote completed constructions; (3) Promote uncompleted constructions; (4) Indicate undeveloped resources. (C) Instill scientific knowledge. (D) Promote the revolutionary spirit. (1) Promote the spirit of sacrifice and struggle; (2) Promote the spirit of hard work and endurance; (3) Promote the spirit of service and creation. (E) Establish national morality.

In their work plan, they also plan to produce educational film scripts, one is textbook-style educational films, and the other is dramatized educational films, but because the cost is huge, it is difficult to implement them temporarily. I believe that in fact, film companies may not be able to produce textbook-style educational films. As for dramatized educational films, film companies can produce them. These educational films are still based on the principles of promoting the national spirit, studying production and construction, instilling scientific knowledge, and establishing national morality, and are not boring and tasteless didactic films. Therefore, dramatized educational films must emphasize both the fun of drama and the significance of education. The recent sound film "Vitality" by Tianyi Company is an example.

"Vitality" depicts a woman's struggle and fully promotes the spirit of "sacrifice, struggle," "hard work, endurance," and "service, creation." It does contain educational significance, but the moving story and the beauty of the techniques are also very rich in dramatic interest. (Feng Ju)

A Corner of the City 276

Yearning for the city seems sweet, but entering the city is like entering a sea of bitterness. According to sociological principles, the city is originally a malformed organization. Needless to say, everything in the city naturally presents a malformed state. Therefore, after we have this understanding of the city, we must conduct an investigation. How can we improve the lives of those already in the city? In other words, what is the inner layer of the city?

It is very clear that in a corner of the city, women who are oppressed by the environment often have a pure heart, ready to enter society to serve and make a living. But what is the result? They are seduced, abandoned, and their bodies are stained with shame that can never be washed away. Women's liberation and equal employment are restrained by demons, and a layer of darkness is added to the city, turning the whole into a pitch-black mass.

Many of my female classmates have left school and flowed into this path. Where has reason gone? They only care about enjoying themselves, and they probably won't wake up until they are old and haggard!

Yesterday, I accompanied my girlfriend to watch the latest Sida Tong sound film "Lipstick Market" by Mingxing. It was truly beyond my expectations. I felt that the consciousness of this film was completely based on the points mentioned above, and it was active, optimistic, and very inspiring to us. At the same time, it is also worthwhile for me to mention and introduce it at the end of this article.

— Xuelu
