Talk

Japanese Planes Flying Over Beiping and All Kinds of Things 277

— Wu

Japanese imperialism can be said to be extremely bold. In China, they have repeatedly formally declared, "If the enemy comes to attack me, I will definitely resist," and that this is a "consistent policy that will never change." Under such a strong attitude, they dare to openly send planes to Beiping to drop bombs after occupying Rehe and Duolun. This not only proves the "atrocities" of Japanese imperialism, but also makes us doubt whether our government's "declarations" are enough to scare the enemy into submission.

On the morning of the 11th, around 7:20, Japanese planes certainly did reconnoiter over Beiping once, and incidentally scattered leaflets. According to a Central News Agency report, "Our troops in the area used anti-aircraft machine guns to fire," so "they did not dare to descend," and even "fled towards Yongdingmen for fear of being shot." Since it is a Central News Agency report, it is certainly very reliable, and the fact that our troops "fired" a volley is enough to increase national prestige. However, according to the same day's Reuters report, "The mystery surrounding the clouds in the sky this morning has deepened even further." The report stated, "The Japanese Embassy claims that it cannot confirm nor deny whether Japanese planes have flown over the skies of Beiping." We certainly do not need to believe the Japanese Embassy's lies, but "the reports from various sources regarding the anti-aircraft artillery are also inconsistent, and even 'foreigners who witnessed it did not hear the sound of artillery.'" This really makes our peace-loving people shake their heads and sigh. Is it necessary for our troops to brag about firing a few cannons? Fortunately, the same report also said, "According to our Air Defense Command, in view of the fact that enemy planes dare to harass Beiping, it has actively deployed air defense measures to protect Chinese and foreign residents. At the same time, the foreign side is deeply dissatisfied with the enemy planes' arbitrary reconnaissance of Beiping, a city and not a military zone, and will raise questions to the Japanese side" (as reported by the Central News Agency on the same day). This way, the people of Beiping can rest assured, and the people of the South can rest even more. Moreover, the above sections can be confirmed by the telegram of the 12th:

1. Enemy planes flew over Beiping again this morning. "Whenever enemy planes flew over the streets, our anti-aircraft artillery machine guns and rifles concentrated their fire." And residents all "looked up from their beds" and can testify.

2. "Enemy planes flew at an altitude of more than 2,000 meters, avoiding our fire."

3. "A shell landed in the courtyard of the actor Zhu Qinxin, fired by our anti-aircraft artillery. A shell also landed on the roof of the Xiaoxia Daily, breaking the tiles."

4. As a result, the enemy planes gained nothing and even "retaliated once," scattering a round of "absurdly worded" leaflets before leaving.

Someone may ask, "Why did our troops only fire from the rooftops and not send up planes for a large-scale air battle?" Then this person is too confused. Didn't Zhang Xueliang go to Mussolini to study the secrets of fascism? Weren't his Ford airplanes given away as gifts? What else is there? Otherwise, there would be no need for Boy Scouts to engage in aviation fundraising on the streets in the sweltering heat.

[P Cat>

— Yu

My wife especially likes cats. After our pet cat drowned last year when I was slightly ill, she got another almost completely white cat. It was snow-white all over, with only two shallow gray spots the size of copper coins on its back. She made a small quilt for it and laid it flat in a specially made wooden box. Every night before going to bed, she would drowsily call it in, gently grab it into the wooden box, and then be able to sleep peacefully. Later, it also knew the scheduled time. When the time came, it didn't need to be called. It would already be sleeping obediently in the wooden box, with its head and limbs curled up together, and its back rising and falling slightly. The shallow gray circle was also quite beautiful, rising and falling. My wife clapped her hands and said, "That cat is really good. People are not as obedient as it!" After saying that, she tilted her head to look at my attitude, as if saying, "Do you know what this means?" At this time, I was probably writing or reading – this has become my habit. After dinner, I always chatted with the people living in the same house. After the cat went to sleep in the wooden box, I realized that it was time for me to write or read. I wouldn't go to sleep until eleven or twelve o'clock. My wife went to sleep very early. When she saw that I wasn't going to sleep early, she said playfully that I wasn't as obedient as the cat. Seeing her tilting her head and smiling triumphantly, I deliberately said, "People are not as smart as cats!" "Yes!" She thought that I didn't know her playfulness and laughed happily.

This cat became a member of our small family.

The spring breeze awakened the earth. One night, the lovely cat disappeared. My wife searched and called everywhere, but she couldn't find it. She said anxiously, "Whoever stole my cat will die a horrible death!"

I knew that after she lost every beloved thing, she would always say that to feel comfortable. That night, she sat silently beside my desk. Unexpectedly, she went to bed with me at one o'clock. In bed, she was still pouting as if she were angry with someone. I gently kissed her lips and said, "What's wrong?" At the same time, a "meow..." sound came from the roof. My wife pushed me away and sat up.

A National Humiliation Commemoration with No Reduction 278

"It's Ah Bai!" she said definitively.

She pushed away the covers, wanting to get out of bed, but I grabbed her hand and said, "Are you going to climb on the roof? It will come back on its own tomorrow!"

"Mew..." The cry gradually approached. This strangely unpleasant "sound" seemed to awaken my wife, who smiled and re-entered the covers. I casually said, "Annoying spring, I'm too lazy to even touch a woman's bottom!"

I received a light punch on my thigh.

The cat's belly slowly swelled, and my wife busied herself preparing a maternity ward. Two weeks ago, it gave birth to two kittens as lovely as their mother. My wife was overjoyed, holding Ah Bai as if she were something precious. The box was moved under our bed, and we watched it nurse. We often held and played with the two kittens. Yesterday, when we returned from the Confucius Temple Park, we didn't know where Ah Bai had moved the two kittens. My wife spoke to Ah Bai as if coaxing a child, but Ah Bai was ultimately not as obedient as a person, and remained confused, not answering. It didn't sleep in the wooden box at night either. I said to my wife:

"You've become a puppet! Once it has children, it forgets you. It's better not to listen!"

"Bah! I'll definitely find it tomorrow."

"Mew..." This morning, the cry came from the roof again. My wife opened the window and looked at Ah Bai, her face showing disappointment.

"Mew..." From this rooftop to that rooftop.

May 11, written before the small building window.

'Paradise' Night 280

— Gan Xiu

This is what people call 'Paradise' Night!

Neon Lights illuminate its dazzling, seductive red and green lights. In the space, glittering buildings stand tall. On the asphalt road, a surging, turbid tide of people and cars flows. So many people are rushing as if they have important matters to attend to! Streams of sweat flow straight down, overflowing with that pungent odor! Disregarding everything!

That mysterious cabaret, filled with the aroma of coffee, emits loud laughter from the door seams: the mellow taste of cocktails; the vibrating melodies of waltzes. Thus, a group of street voyeurs crane their necks, peeping and eavesdropping, with expressions of envious jealousy, tirelessly waiting until the uniformed patrolman treats them with a wooden club!

Outside, on the bustling sidewalk, many frivolous young men, like bees and butterflies, follow behind every young and beautiful woman, whistling lewdly and flirting passionately. Then, the young and pretty girls return a flirtatious glance and a clever smile; or they curse softly, pretending to scold!

Moreover, in the shadows of quiet buildings, a contrasting tragedy is being enacted upside down. Look! Behind every man, whether white-haired, grown-up, frail, strong, well-dressed, or simply attired, there always follows one or more women: plaster faces, dull eyes, stiff, corpse-like bodies. An old madam follows them gloomily. When the arc lights of a speeding car flash across their thin faces, every face remains expressionless!

In order to satisfy the greed of the madams, to satiate the animalistic desires of men, and for their own survival, they are forced to endure the extreme punishment of being slowly sliced to pieces. There is no joy or comfort. The stones of misfortune circle above their heads, and those stones strike their heads at any time and any place. When they lose the last of their youthful beauty, that is the moment when the stone of misfortune strikes them fatally.

At this time, perhaps someone is praising the greatness of the metropolis, and especially the greatness of the metropolis at night!

And coincidentally, hidden within the atmosphere of this great city's night is a tragic and cruel fate!

This is what people call 'Paradise' Night!

Male Students in Shanghai 281

— Er Chu

I remember a few days ago, someone wrote an article in this journal called "Female Students in Shanghai," which was extremely thorough. I am simply writing an article called "Male Students in Shanghai" to promote gender equality. Mimicking others is inevitable.

The term "male student" evokes a mystical fantasy, especially among middle school and university students. Indeed, those neatly dressed in Western suits and leather shoes, carrying original Western books several inches thick under their arms... Ah! All of that quickly floods into the mind.

Parents spend huge sums of money to send them to school, and the nation cultivates them earnestly. What is the purpose? What exactly do they do at school to live up to themselves and others? Have they recognized this turbulent era? Have they shouldered the important current mission they should bear?

Alas! It is painful to say! Most male students are still fooling around with themselves. Needless to say, they are deceiving themselves and others. They waste a lot of money in vain, and the result is that they gain nothing. Instead, they become infected with the extravagant and wasteful Europeanized habits, and they also have a conceited heart. Their will is weakened, their spirit is scattered, and they remain drunk and numb, passing their days like walking corpses. When they have nothing to do, they either play a few decadent tunes or hum a few nauseating poems. Running around to movie theaters and dance halls is their daily life. When they can't stand living, they "commit suicide" a few times, and they can be called "patriotic suicides" and show off their "death." As for what they learn and what the national crisis is, they can put it all behind them and wait to have some fun before talking about it (?) because the Japanese devils are still far away in the north!

A few good-looking and beautiful students also do some "anti-Japanese association" things, giving a speech on the podium; of course, they are righteous and confident, and the audience is shocked. They say "go to the national crisis together" and "young students can no longer be numb"... After leaving the podium, they remain the same. They still go to the dance hall to watch movies in the evening. They are not ashamed to be the leaders of "saving the country with movies" and "saving the country with dancing" (?)

Occasionally, the damned professor wants to give a surprise test, which is terrible! It really worries our young master students. They can only pretend to be Liu Bei for the time being. But it doesn't matter, after a while, they are Zhang Fei on the sports field!

Oh! Students are the future masters of the country? They are the backbone of society? They are the leaders who lead the people? They are the pioneers of political reform? They are... Alas! Great male students! I want to be speechless!

Suffering After Early Marriage 282

Announcements for this Column 283

It is understood that the purpose of setting up this column is to assist workers, shop assistants, apprentices, etc. in solving difficult problems. In the case of the letter writer, they should be satisfied with receiving a reply; in the past two months, thanks to the support of all sectors, there have been more than a dozen inquiries per day. Although we have the ambition to answer every letter, we are limited by facts. In addition to the common problems that we believe everyone has, which are published in the newspaper every day, the remaining problems that are specific to individuals will be answered directly by this column in a letter. However, we have received many letters in recent days that have not clearly stated the address in accordance with the rules. It is presumed that their intention is simply to hope to be published in the newspaper; however, a detailed analysis of the content of the problems does not have much to do with the general public. If we follow the instructions and publish them one by one, not only will readers inevitably lose interest, but there is no space to accommodate thirteen or fourteen letters per day. It is hoped that future letters will be handled in accordance with the regulations of this column, especially the address must be clearly stated, otherwise, we will not reply, please understand.

Regulations for the Shop Assistant Communication Column

(1) The purpose of communication is to gather ideas, explain difficult problems, learn from each other, and increase the happiness of life.

(2) The target of communication is limited to shop assistants, apprentices, and workers, and only limited to this port.

(3) Communication content: Everything about personal daily life, such as:

(1) Occupation (2) Moral and academic cultivation (3) Entertainment and sports (4) Marriage, as well as other issues related to the country and society, are all welcome. If the content of the problem is too profound and beyond the capabilities of this column, it can also be introduced to the "Reader Advisory" of this newspaper for answering.

(4) Letter Writing Method

(1) The name, age, native place, occupation, and detailed correspondence address must be clearly stated at the end of the letter; it must still be stated when continuing to write letters.

(2) The writing style of the letter is not limited, but it should be simple and easy to understand, and it must be written clearly.

(3) Please write the words "Shop Assistant Communication Column, Supplementary Publication, Shenbao Museum, this port" on the envelope: if you need a reply, please also attach a two-cent stamp.

(4) Communicators must cut off the special printed stamp of this column and paste it on the upper left corner of the letter, otherwise, it will not be answered.

(5) Handling Method After Receiving a Letter

(1) If the newspaper believes that the problem being discussed has value for the public, it may be disclosed in the newspaper.

(2) In order to respect the opinions of the communicator, if the letter states that they do not want their name to be disclosed, or that they need a separate response, it can also be handled accordingly.

(3) If the communicator hopes to disclose the letter in the newspaper, but cannot disclose the full text due to excessive length, it should be published selectively. If the content of the problem is complicated and has to be carefully studied, so that the answer or disclosure is delayed, please understand.

(4) When there are a lot of letters, the answers will be given in the order in which the letters were received, and please understand if there is any delay.

Novel

The Life of the Five Concubines (9) (Continued) 284

— Ling He

She looked towards the bed, Grandpa Zhang was still sleeping like a pig. Originally, she should have gone over to get a blanket to cover him, but because she was too lazy to move, she let it go.

At some point, Grandpa Zhang finally woke up. He was bound to give his little beauty sleeping next to him some gentle care, and naturally said a lot of sweet words, but Miss Liu did not seem to be moved in any way, which was naturally very disappointing. But Grandpa Zhang always had good intentions, and the most obvious was his determination to rescue her from this brothel's fire pit. The solution was that he himself only had a wife of many years, and according to his status, he should have a concubine. So Miss Liu was naturally sufficient to occupy this position.

Miss Liu listened very carefully to the passionate words. Logically, she should have been excited, but she was unwilling to specifically state her opinion, always responding with "Hum, hum, hum." This directly made our Grandpa Zhang unable to figure out what was going on. Afterwards, Miss Liu stayed awake until dawn. Probably because of insomnia, her head was very swollen and painful. She struggled to get up, drank a cup of cold tea, and walked to the window, looking at the gray sky. She sighed heavily, thinking in her heart:

"Alright, I'll just marry him."

(9) In Happiness

Since Miss Liu agreed to Grandpa Zhang's request that night, after several negotiations, Miss Liu actually married over.

According to Wu Gui, Miss Liu did not seem particularly happy about this matter. However, Mother Yang from the brothel took this opportunity to make a fortune, which was true. Not to mention anything else, in terms of her value alone, the original asking price was 1,200 yuan, but Grandpa Zhang was only willing to pay 600. Of course, the difference was too much. In the end, it was agreed that 800 yuan would be paid. However, there were also the four-color gifts that Grandpa Zhang sent to Mother Yang, which were not included: a fox fur coat, a pair of large gold earrings... Although they were all readily available to Grandpa Zhang, and he only had to take them from his own pawnshop, but calculated, they were also worth two or three hundred yuan. However, every time Mother Yang talked to others, she always said that she was doing good deeds and didn't want to ruin a young girl, so she sold her off cheaply. If she had kept her for a few more years, she was sure that she could have made a lot of money.

But there are really things in the world that make it impossible to understand the reason. For example, Grandpa Zhang spent so much money to marry Miss Liu this time, and logically, he should cherish her like a treasure. However, in fact, it was not so. Apart from sleeping in her room from time to time for more than a month at the beginning, he did not take her with him when he took office this time. Of course, Grandma Zhang had quarreled several times about this matter, and it was said that she had smashed the jade-inlaid clock in anger. But if Grandpa Zhang insisted on taking Miss Liu with him, what method could Grandma Zhang use to stop him? Besides, she was already almost fifty years old and had never given birth to a son or daughter. Grandpa Zhang could use this as a reason. Could Miss Liu pass on the family line for the Zhang family if she didn't see Grandpa Zhang for many years? So Grandpa Zhang really didn't put her entirely in his heart.

Film Special

Basic Knowledge of Film Appreciation 285

— Yao Yinzhong

There is no doubt that film today is enthusiastically welcomed and loved by the general public, forming a universal trend; and the development of the domestic film industry is not inferior to that of foreigners, which is especially gratifying. It is only a pity that the general public's knowledge of appreciation seems to be somewhat lacking. I am now sharing my personal experience in watching movies with you, with the intention of discussing it with everyone.

Regardless of any film, its establishment conditions are four, namely:

(1) Script: The essence of film is also one of drama, it naturally needs a script like other dramas; the value of a film is very related to the quality of the script, so only a good script can have a great film; this goes without saying. The establishment conditions for a script are also two: one is the theme, and the other is the consciousness. The theme is the element that constitutes the script, and the consciousness can be said to be its skeleton. What we should pay attention to here are these two items.

(2) Actors: With a script, but without actors, there is no way to produce a film. And a good film also needs good actors to perform; the so-called good actors, of course, must have sufficient cultivation in film. What we should pay attention to here is whether the role played by the actor in the film is suitable, and whether the performance skills are flawless; most importantly, whether they can fully express the personality of the character.

(3) Director: With a script and actors, there is still a need to allocate and arrange, and to instruct the performance, which is the responsibility of the so-called "director." His position and authority in the film are also imaginable. Some people compare him to the commander-in-chief of the army, which is very appropriate. Therefore, whether a film is good or bad is closely related to him; the famous and expensive films in Europe and the United States are all created by directors with superb skills. What we should pay attention to here, of course, is his overall design skills for this film; as for skills and techniques, they should also be paid attention to at the same time.

(4) Photography: The script is arranged, the actors are assigned, and they have performed. After that, it is to capture them in the lens. Only when the work reaches this level is it considered complete; the so-called "photographer" works under the control of the director, and his duties include the "lighting," "subtitles," "pictures," "background," and "characters" of the film. And what we should pay attention to here is these.

In addition, now is the era of sound films, and attention should also be paid to its "music," "singing," and "dialogue." We must put effort into appreciating these aspects, and we must not ignore one or two points; otherwise, we cannot be considered to have done our best in appreciation. Finally, I must also tell everyone that we must recognize that film is also art, and it is also scientific art. (Thanks)

Film Review

Review of "Strictly Personal" 286

— Yan Nan

I have a kind of inexplicable fondness for Paramount's productions. Although I dare not say that every one of their films is good. But most of them are not bad. There are very few that fail. "Strictly Personal," although the whole film can't really find anything particularly good, at the same time, it can't be said that there is anything bad. Everything is just walking along the horizontal line.

The story in American films should be considered superior. There are no golden dreams here, only a very common phenomenon in society. However, if it is not a mistake by the screenwriter, then the director should be responsible. The film as a whole generally does not have anything that is unreasonable, but in the details, there are some omissions, and there is a very vague consciousness in the story, which seems to be not very coherent from beginning to end. Briefly speaking, it tells the story of an old couple who, because they had been in prison, were quite repentant after escaping, and set up a small club in a small town with a friend's daughter. Unexpectedly, a thug came and threatened to report the escape, intending to seize the club. The old couple had no choice but to agree to share the profits with him. The thug soon committed a murder case for money, and shifted the blame to the old couple. Fortunately, the evidence was not accurate, and they were released. The thug then seduced the old couple's friend's daughter, intending to go to Mexico together. At the airport, the thug was suddenly shot and killed. A young reporter who had been in love with the girl then returned home with her.

The instructions were translated inaccurately, and the meaning of the play lacked a center. There was too much dialogue during the performance, sometimes a lot of nonsense that did not address the topic. For example, who killed the thug was never explained clearly, and for example, the girl's father was released, and the girl took refuge in the small club. All the actors' performances were very conflicted and inhumane.

The court's treatment of the murder case was very light, which was actually to accommodate the ending of the whole play, and it did not hesitate to place the spirit of the law in the background. There was also a description of the American reporters' boredom, annoyance, and embarrassment, which was very incisive, making people laugh and pity.

To put it in fashionable terms, the dialogue is very "humorous"... Although there is not a single comedian, there are not a few jokes. The director has also done his best in terms of scene division and presentation. Photography, lighting, sound recording, location, and arrangement... According to the performance standards of American films, it is only average.

In terms of performance, the old woman Marjorie Rambeau is the protagonist, and her expressions are mostly superior and commendable. However, Dorothy Jordan's performance in the whole film is the best, very much like a naive girl.

Review of "Flower of Peace": A Small Company's Production Is Commendable 287

Since the closure of Youlian Company last winter, more than half of the actors and staff have switched to Mingxing Company. However, from 1930 to the summer of 1932, more than ten films were made in two years. But for reasons such as reorganization, they have not been publicly screened. Recently, the liquidation office of Youlian Company has started to close down, so all the films have been cleared out in order to clear the principal and interest of each shareholder. "Flower of Peace" is the first of those films in storage.

Youlian produced "Yu Meiren" in the winter of 1930, which was also the first sound film made in China. Later, it used Erde's great book "Wild River Heroine" as a selling point. But this "Flower of Peace," half sound and half martial arts (?), actually changed to a new style, and the story is also extremely novel. There are many allusions in it. For example, Peace Valley clearly represents China, Jinyue represents a certain warlord; Gu Guosi refers to the Chinese people; Fu Li is said to be Puyi... People who have seen this film will definitely be very clear.

The outline of the story: Peace Valley was unfortunately occupied by the strong neighbor Jinyue. One of the villagers, Gu Guosi, plotted resistance but failed. The daughter of the old village chief, who was studying abroad, later returned to the valley, and the village chief had been killed. So she contacted her comrades and vowed to avenge her father. The villagers pushed Gu Guosi as the leader, responding from the inside and outside, killing Jinyue and driving out all the bandits, and Hanmin, the general who defected from Jinyue's command, and the daughter of the old village chief became a loving couple.

It is easy to see the director's skills during the performance. The scene division, etc., are all impeccable. There is also considerable success in photography. The lighting is still mostly exterior, so it is completely using sunlight. There are only two small segments in which the characters are too dark because the focal point of the lens is not suitable. There are very few omissions and gaps. It is rare for a production of a small company to be like this.

A scene from the Wufa Gaomeng co-production "Peach Blossom Village," Jacques Hollander and Sunny Hale are courting Zerlene Harville, which is a musical and singing film with nature as the background, scheduled to be released at the Nanjing Grand Theater on Wednesday of this week.

A big regret is that the director raided the old tricks of martial arts films, which backfired. The insertion of large segments of chaotic fighting is really like children fighting. Thirty or forty villagers and twenty or thirty bandit gangs, the so-called large force, are just that, which is too childish. The sword fighting is the same as the full martial arts on the stage, specializing in falling, which is a pity.

The overall performance is mediocre. Bao Gusong is slightly better, and Ye Juanjuan's few scenes are also moving. Xu Qinfang's martial arts are very good, but her expression is naive. Below Zi Kui, it is even less worth mentioning.

This film is produced by a small Chinese company, so I would like to introduce it to everyone to see.

"Peach Blossom Village" Worth Introducing 288

— Xin Fu

Premiering this Wednesday in Nanjing

The De-Ying Film Company's joint production, "Spring River in the Flower Moon Night," has already caused a sensation among Chinese and foreign film fans in Shanghai. Now, this long-awaited film, "Peach Blossom Village" (Happy Ever After), jointly produced by Wufa and Gaumont, will premiere this Wednesday at the Nanjing Grand Theater. This is the latest work of Ulrich Promayr, the film production giant of Wufa. The films he produces always have something special. This "Peach Blossom Village" is certainly no exception.

It is a film depicting a segment of petty-bourgeois life. Its structure is completely different from "Spring River in the Flower Moon Night." Because "Spring River in the Flower Moon Night" only introduces to the screen pleasing songs, melodious music, lighthearted humor, and soft, beautiful scenery; while "Peach Blossom Village," in addition to possessing the above conditions, has achieved extraordinary success in the progress of the story and the vividness of the performances.

Lilian Harvey, who gained fame from "Dragon Soaring Phoenix Dancing" and was hired by the United States for a large sum, plays a homeless village girl in this film. The London New Century Newspaper said that her performance has never been as moving as in this "Peach Blossom Village." Jack Hulbert and Sonny Hale play a couple of silly young men here. One was the protagonist of "Happy Marriage," which premiered at Carlton last year; the other has already met us in "Spring River in the Flower Moon Night," and various newspapers have said that he is the one with the best expressions. These three stars gathered together. How good the result will be, we can already imagine.

Movie Novel Secrets (10) 289

— Cairo

John's hot tears were already streaming down, and he said, "This really makes me ashamed to the extreme, with no place to hide. But what about the future? My reputation is lost, I am rejected by society, and although you forgive me, my children will also despise their father."

"John, John," Mary's voice was again full of the spirit of encouraging progress, "Stand up, muster your courage, and restore your usual spirit! When we had no hope before, we were still able to fight to the end and win. The war ahead of us will be even more difficult than what we have experienced before. But if the two of us can work together and strive forward, victory will still belong to us!"

"Work together! Work together!" John repeated. From then on, the two of them worked together to strive forward. Year after year, until his reputation was restored and he saw the light of day again. John's reputation was even greater than before. John had been a senator for several years. However, for several years, because John was diligent in public affairs from morning till night, the affection between the couple became estranged. John knew that Mary had long harbored fear and pain in her heart, so he decided not to continue as a senator, willing to use the remaining years of his life to make up for the loss of his beloved wife.

But now there are obstacles and enemies in front of them. These obstacles and enemies are none other than their own children. They rely on the results of their parents' lifelong struggle, enjoying comfort. When their parents are old, they still do not allow them to retire because of their selfish and self-serving hearts. Therefore, when John announced his intention not to continue as a senator, a group of children quarreled, protested, and opposed John's withdrawal from politics. Seeing this, John was very angry and said, "You really annoy us!"

A group of children looked at each other, feeling very surprised. Mary hurriedly explained to her children, "Children, don't misunderstand your father's meaning. How can we bear to part with you, having been together with you day and night for decades? But we have used half of our lives' souls on you, and now that you are all grown up and can be independent, we cannot not take back our souls." "Mother," the eldest son William said, "I simply don't understand what you're saying."

"You won't understand. We have our secrets." John answered for Mary.

"Secrets?" the second son, Robert, said in great surprise. "Do you have any secrets from us too?"

"That's right, Robert," Mary explained to him. "We have our secrets, you won't know them. Perhaps there is a kind of secret between husband and wife that others cannot understand. Your father and I certainly also have our own secrets. Secret joys, secret worries, lovely secrets, painful secrets. Only your father and I can share them together." "Come," John said to Mary. The two of them then took hands and entered their bedroom. Outside, the children were still shouting and arguing. But John and Mary had already secretly prepared, slipped out through a secret door, and took a car to a secret place. (The End)
